namāmi vigrahaṃ sāmvaṃ saṃsāraviṣabheṣajam
satrāvasāne saṃnadvāḥ sarvavedārthavedane
sarvalokahite yuktāḥ sārāsāravivekinaḥ
svādhyāyādhyayane yuktāḥ svasthacittāḥ suniścalāḥ
abhyāgatānāmārtānāmatithīnāṃ priyaṃvadāḥ
maitryā karuṇayā yuktāḥ kumatāvapyupekṣakāḥ
parapuṣṭau mahāprītāḥ prajñāmānavivarjitāḥ
gavāṃ śuśrūṣaṇe yuktā guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥ
vṛddhasevābhisaṃpannā vedavitpūjane ratāḥ
ṛjavo mṛdavaḥ svasthāḥ sarvadvaṃdvavivarjitāḥ
rudrākṣamālābharaṇāḥ sitamasmāvaguṇṭhitāḥ
tripuṇḍāvalibhirdīptā jaṭāvalkalasaṃyutāḥ
liṅgārcanaparā nityaṃ śivasyāmitatejasaḥ
śivābhimānasaṃpannāḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ
śivaśabdajapadhvastapāpapañjarasundarāḥ
saṃsāravipavṛkṣasya mūlacchedanatatparāḥ
śrautasmārta sadācārāḥ sarvagotrarpayo varāḥ
vyāsaprasādasaṃpannaṃ viśvajñānamahodadhim
viśvātmavedinaṃ sākṣādvidhvastabhavakānanam
smṛtvā bhaktyā mahātmānaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ sūtamuttamam
etasminnantare śrīmānmahākāruṇikottamaḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvabhūtānāmabhīṣṭaphaladaḥ prabhuḥ
prādurāsīnmahātejā rātrau sūrya iva svayam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ sarve vismitā gadradasvarāḥ
praṇamya daḍavaḍūmau dattvā tasyā''sanaṃ varam
pādaprakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā śraddhayā parayā saha
gandhapuṣpādibhirdivyaiḥ pūṃjya puṇyavatāṃ varam
samāśvāsya ciraṃ kālaṃ prasannamukhapaṅkajam
so'pi sūtaḥ svamācāryai smṛtvā śaṃbhuṃ jagadgurum
sarvavidyāmayīmīśāṃ sākṣādvighnavināyakam
ṣaṇmukhaṃ ca sadā śuddhaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṇḍavat
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā munīnālokya suvratān
namāmi saṃsāramahāviṣauṣadham
atha vakṣyāmi vedārthe śṛṇuta śraddhayā dvijāḥ
parāparavibhāgena vedārtho dvividhaḥ smṛtaḥ
vedārthaḥ paramaḥ sākṣātparātparataraṃ param
gīyate muniśārdūlaiḥ kadācinna tu mukhyataḥ
avyākulena dharmeṇa śraddhayā'nuṣṭhitena tu
vedārthaḥ paramaḥ sākṣātsidhyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
ekaiva paramā śaktirmāyā durghaṭakāriṇī
śivasyānantarūpā sā vidyayā tasya naśyati
yā vinaśyati sā māyā cinmātre parikalpitā
adhiṣṭhānāvaśeṣo hi nāśaḥ kalpitavastunaḥ
bhāvasyaiva hyabhāvatvaṃ nāśo'bhāvasya bhavataḥ
bhāvābhāvasvabhāvābhyāmanya eva hi kelpitaḥ
adhiṣṭhānasya nāśo na satyatvādeva sarvadā
sarvādhiṣṭhānamīśānaṃ paśyanneva vimucyate
īśānaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ vedāntaśravaṇādinā
jāyate parahaṃsasya yatermukhyādhikāriṇaḥ
nā''śramāntaraniṣṭhasya kramāttasyāpi jāyate
gṛhasthaḥ pitṛlokaṃ ca śivajñānaṃ tu bhikṣukaḥ
mahāpāpādayatnena mucyate munipuṅgavāḥ
dvitīyaḥ śāntidāntyādijñānānecchāmavāpnuyāt
tṛtīyo'khilavedāntaśravaṇecchāmavāmuyāt
caturtho jñānamāproti vedāntaśravaṇena tu
sa eva karmasaṃnyāsī parahaṃsasamāśrayaḥ
anye kāmyaparityāgādvikṣukā iti kīrtitāḥ
parokṣaṃ brahmavijñānaṃ śābdaṃ deśikapūrvakam
buddhipūrvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dahati vahnivat
śābdaṃ brahmātmavijñānamaparokṣaṃ mahattaram
saṃsāranāśakaṃ proktaṃ tamasaścaṇḍabhānuvat
ato vijñānalābhāya parahaṃso bhaveddijaḥ
kuṭīcakāśca haṃsāśva tathā'nye ca bahūkāḥ
ye bhaviṣyanti te kuryuḥ prājāpatyeṣṭisaṃjñitām
āgneyeṣṭiṃ dvijāḥ kuryuḥ parahaṃsābhilāṣiṇaḥ
paścātraidhātavīṃ kuryuḥ sarve saṃyatamānasāḥ
ye'nāhitāgnayo viprāsteṣāṃ neṣṭirvidhīyate
hutaśeṣaṃ caruṃ sājyaṃ prāśyā''camyaiva sarpiṣā
pūrṇāhutiṃ punaḥ kuryuḥ praṇavenāgnijāyayā
sahāniṃ punarāmrāya ayaṃ te yonirṛtvijaḥ
saṃnyāsādhvaryuṇā dattaṃ daṇḍaṃ kāpāyameva ca
parigṛhya guroḥ pādaṃ praṇamya śraddhayā saha
vedāntaśravaṇaṃ kuryurjñānārthaṃ bhikṣukottamāḥ
trayīsāramimaṃ mantraṃ jaṃpennityaṃ samāhitaḥ
praṇavādaparaṃ jatthā kadā mukto bhaviṣyati
oṅkāraḥ sarvamantrāṇāmuttamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
oṅkāreṇa lavenaiva saṃsārābdhi tariṣyati
umārdhavigraho devo rudraḥ satyādilakṣaṇaḥ
viṣṇvādayo'pi devāśca rudrasyāsyānvayena tu
sthānaṃ saṃsevanīyaṃ syāñcintanīyaṃ tathaiva ca
avimukte mahādevaḥ sākṣādiśveśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
upāsyamānaḥ suprīto jñānaṃ sākṣātprayacchati
naraḥ kiṃcidipaṃ bhuktvā kṣunivṛttiṃ kariṣyati
rudrajāpī vimucyeta mahāpātakapañjarāva
anena sadṛśaṃ japyaṃ nāsti satyaṃ śrutau smṛtau
epā pañcākṣarī vidyā śatarudriyamadhyagā
pañcākṣare mahādevaḥ sarvadā supratiṣṭhitaḥ
mahādevasya sāṃnidhyādvyaṣṭibhūtāśva devatāḥ
tatra pratiṣṭhitā eva vṛkṣe śākhā yathā sthitāḥ
vṛkṣasya mūlasekena śākhāḥ puṣyanti vai yathā
śive rudrajapātprīte prītā evānyadevatāḥ
māyā māheśvarī śaktiḥ sattvādiguṇabhedataḥ
jīvamākramya saṃsāre bhrāmayatyaniśaṃ dvijāḥ
sattvātsukhaṃ ca jñānaṃ ca vairāgyaṃ śauklyameva ca
'evamuttamarūpāśca padārthāḥ sattvasaṃbhavāḥ
tathā madhyamarūpāśca padārthā rājasāḥ smṛtāḥ
vihīnāstāmasā eva padārthāḥ saṃgraheṇa tu
ato māyāmayaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām
jñānayajñena viprāṇāmāstikānāmamāninām
jāyate paramaṃ jñānaṃ nānyathā munipuṅgavāḥ
yajñaśca dvividhaḥ proktaḥ sthūlasūkṣmaṃvibhedataḥ
karmayajñaḥ samākhyātaḥ sthūlaḥ sarvārthavittamaiḥ
jñānayajño bhavetsūkṣmaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāravādhakaḥ
kāyiko vācikaścaiva mānasaśceti suvratāḥ
mantrāṇāṃ japarūpastu vāciko vedavittamāḥ
devatādhyānarūpastu mānasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
kāyikādādhikaḥ prokto vāciko matimattaḥ
mānaso vācikācchreṣṭha mānaso bahudhā smṛtaḥ
viṣṇvādīnāṃ tu devānāṃ dhyānaṃ cādhamamipyate
ato mokṣārthibhiḥ prājñaiḥ śiva aikaḥ śivaṃkaraḥ
asminnarthe śrutiḥ sādhvī samāptā vedavittamāḥ
apakvacittairmokṣārthaṃ devā viṣṇvādayo'pi ca
dhyeyāḥ pakkaiḥ śivo dhyeyaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāramocakaḥ
rudraṃ viśvādhikaṃ viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇaṃ cānyameva vā
samaṃ saṃcintayansākṣātsaṃsāre parivartate
mahāpāpavatāṃ puṃsāṃ pūrvajanmasu suvratāḥ
viṣṇuḥ sarvādhiko bhāti na sākṣātparameśvaraḥ
viṣṇuḥ sarvādhiko bhāti nārakī sa na saṃśayaḥ
viṣṇuḥ sarvādhiko nāmya iti cintayatāṃ nṛṇām
nāsti saṃsāravicchittiḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi
tepāṃ naiva ca mokṣāśā kalpakoṭiśatairapi
brahmādidevatānāṃ ca viśvādhikyaṃ vadanti ye
sāmyaṃ vadanti ye teṣāṃ na saṃsārādvimokṣaṇam
viṣṇuprajāpatīndrādidevatāsu munīśvarāḥ
vihīnāsu śivaṃ paśyanmucyate bhavabandhanāt
śivarudra mahādevabrahmeśānādināmataḥ
viṣṇvādidevatāḥ paśyankramānmucyeta bandhanāt
śivaṃ sarvottamaṃ viprā hariviṣṇvādināmataḥ
yathā'mātyādibuddhistu rājñi bādhāya dehinām
tathā viṣṇvādibuddhistu śive vādhāya dehinām
ataḥ śivaḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ prādhānyena manīṣibhiḥ
jñānayajñātparo yajño nāsti nāsti śrutau smṛtau
mahāpāpavatāṃ nṛṇāṃ jñānayajño na rocate
viśuddhaṃ jñānamutpannaṃ yasya tasya mahātmanaḥ
śivarudramahādevabrahmeśānādināmasu
rudramūrtiṣu sarvāsu śāntidāntyādisādhane
tiryaktrapuṇḍre rudrākṣe tathā bhasmāvaguṇṭhane
śivaliṅgasya prajāyāṃ śivasthāneṣu suvratāḥ
upekṣā vā na sa jñānī paśurvijñānavañcakaḥ
rutkarṣādityato viṣṇvādiṣu śivabuddhiryuktetyāha viṣṇuprajāpatīti
sākṣāddijñānino viprā upekṣābuddhireva hi
tathā'pyukteṣu sarveṣu śaiveṣu dvijapuṅgavāḥ
priyabuddhiḥ svato bhāti vādhitākārarūpataḥ
epvasau naiva vijñānī bhrānta eva na saṃśayaḥ
jñānāvalambanenaiva jīvantyanye vimohitāḥ
mayā madguruṇā'nyairvā na śakyaṃ paribhāṣitum
tathā'pi munayaḥ śraddhāmātramāsādya kevalam
praśaṃsanti mahābhāgyājjñānayajñasya vaibhavam
aśaktā api vijñātuṃ jñānayajñasya vaibhavam
śraddhayā svādhikāreṇa vadanti jñānavaibhavam
punaḥ kaṇādakapilaprabhṛtīnāmapi svataḥ
upacāreṇa vijñānaṃ śraddhāpratatayā dvijāḥ
vyāsaḥ sākṣācchivajñānī śivasyaiva prasādataḥ
tatprasādādahaṃ sākṣācchivajñānī na saṃśayaḥ
mayā tatsaṃgraheṇaiva proktaṃ yuṣmākamādarāt
matprasādena vijñānayajñavaibhavamāstikāḥ
jñātavantaḥ kṛtārthāśca yūyaṃ satyamidaṃ vacaḥ
itaḥ pūrva mayā'nyeṣāṃ nāyamartho'bhibhāṣitaḥ
vyāso mama guruḥ pūrva rahasyaṃ me'bhyabhāṣata
sārātsārataraḥ sākṣādayamarthaḥ prabhāṣitaḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sutasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ
nāma dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ
karmayajñavidhā prokto munibhiḥ sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ
prādhānyena phalaṃ śuddhirārthikī kāmyakarmaṇaḥ
kāmyarūpeṣu yajñeṣu yatante śraddhayā saha
mahābhāgyāḥ pravartante teṣāṃ muktirayatnataḥ
aiṣu yajñeṣu sarveṣu teṣāṃ mandaphalaṃ bhavet
śivārādhanavṛddhayā ye yatante śraddhayā saha
eṣu yajñeṣu te śīghraṃ vimuktiphalamāpnuyuḥ
akartā'hamabhoktā'hamasaṅgo'hamahaṃ śivaḥ
iti vijñāya mānena svātmānaṃ tarkato'pi caṃ
karmayajñeṣu ye nityaṃ yatante śraddhayā'nvitāḥ
mahādevavijñānamaparokṣamavāpnuyuḥ
yajñarūpaṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ yajñe paśyanti ye dvijāḥ
te tu vijñānamāsādya kaivalyaṃ jñānamāpnuyuḥ
prādhānyena mahādevo yajñairijyo na cāparaḥ
iti jñātvā yajante ye te'pi vijñānamāpnuyuḥ
viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇamindraṃ vā devatāntarameva vā
te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
nāmataścārthato yastu mahādevo maheśvaraḥ
sa eva sāmbaḥ sarvajña ijyaḥ sarvamahāmakhaiḥ
yāni loke'niṣiddhāni karmāṇyavihitāni ca
tāni śaṃbho mahāpūjetye tajjñānaṃ mahāmakhaḥ
yāni karmāṇi sarvāṇi niṣiddhāni śrutau smṛtau
tāni cā''rādhanaṃ śaṃbhoriti jñānaṃ mahāmakhaḥ
īśvarārthadhiyā pāpānyapi karmāṇi suvratāḥ
ārdrakāṣṭhaṃ mahānagniḥ śuṣkaṃ kṛtvā dahedyathā
tatheśvaradhiyā pāpaṃ śuddhavijñānadaṃ bhavet
vidhyuktakarmaniṣṭhānāmiṣṭasya karaṇaṃ tu yat
so'pi sākṣānmahāyajñaḥ samyagjñānasya kāraṇam
vidhyuktakarmaniṣṭhānāmaniṣṭakaraṇaṃ tu yat
durācāriṣu sarveṣu vinā doṣasya darśanam
upekṣāvṛddhirutpannoṃ so tasyāyaṃ mahāmakhaḥ
devatābudvimātraṃ yatso'pi yajñaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
vaidikaṃ tāntrikaṃ hitvā mārga svaprajñayā dvijāḥ
āstikyaṃ devatābuddhirapi lābhāya dehinām
phaleṣu tāratamyaṃ tu vidyate sūkṣmadarśane
kāyikaḥ karmayajñastu kathitaḥ saṃgraheṇa tu
bhavanto'pi mahāyajñaṃ kāyikaṃ kuruta dvijāḥ
karmayajñavaibhavanirūpaṇaṃ nāma tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ
karmayajñavaibhavanirūpaṇaṃ nāma tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ
athāhaṃ vācikaṃ yajñaṃ vakṣyāmi śraddhayā saha
parātparatarāttasmācchivāccaitanyalakṣaṇāva
śabdaḥ sūkṣmaḥ svabhāvena prādurāsīdakhaṇḍitaḥ
sa śabdaḥ punarādhāre prāṇināmāstikottamāḥ
piṇḍībhūtatayā''bhāti taptajāmbūnadaprabhaḥ
vibhaktaḥ sūkṣmarūpeṇa bhāti vahnipremaḥ svataḥ
piṇḍībhūtatayā prāpya prakāśānandalakṣaṇe
tatra saṃnihite śaṃbho viśrāntiṃ labhate svataḥ
ādhāre paraśaktestu sthāne śabdaḥ prakāśitaḥ
paramekākṣaraṃ sākṣādbhavatyatyantaśobhanam
ājñāsaṃjñānmahāsthānādūrdhvaṃ yatsthānamuttamam
tatrastho'yaṃ dvijāḥ śabdaḥ sūkṣmekākṣaratāmiyāt
tṛtīye paramādhāre pūrake puṇyabhājane
ekākāratvamāproti svabhāvenākṣaradvayam
mananatrāṇarūpatvānmantra ityabhiśabditaḥ
mātṛkā paramā devī mantramātā maheśvarī
asmādādyānmahāmantrādāvirbhūtā svabhāvataḥ
tasmācchrīmātṛkā śṛddhā cāṃ''dyamantrātmikī bhavet
mananatrāṇarūpatvānmantra ityabhiśabditaḥ
mātṛkā paramā devī mantramātā maheśvarī
asmādādyānmahāmantrādāvirbhūtā svabhāvataḥ
tasmācchrī mātṛkā śuddhā cā''dyamantrātmikī bhavet
gurūpadeśato jñeyo nānyathā śāstrakoṭibhiḥ
svaprakāśasvarūpasya vācako'yaṃ paro manuḥ
tricaturvatsaraṃ śiṣyaṃ parīkṣya satataṃ punaḥ
īśvarādeśato deyo mantro'yaṃ mantrisattamaiḥ
aparīkṣya pradānena śīghraṃ mṛtyumavāpnuyāt
asya mantrasya vaiśiṣṭayaṃ mayā vaktuṃ na śakyate
mantrāṇāṃ mātṛbhūtā ca mātṛkā parameśvarī
sā punaḥ kramabhedena mahāmantrātmanā tathā
mantrātmanā ca vedādiśabdākāreṇa ca svataḥ
satyetareṇa śabdenāpyāvirbhavati suvratāḥ
yathā parataraḥ śaṃbhurvidhā śaktiśivātmanā
tathaiva mātṛkā devī dvidhābhūtā bhavetsvayam
ekākāreṇa śaktestu vācakaśvetareṇa tu
śivasya vācakaḥ sākṣādvidheyaṃ padagāminī
apadaṃ padamāpanaṃ padaṃ cāpyapadaṃ bhavet
padāpadavibhāṃgaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati
padasthasya jitā mantrā bhaveyuḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ
padābhyāsaparāṇāṃ tu na kiṃcidapi durlabham
aṃśa ekaḥ padasyāyamupakārāya dehinām
bhavetpoḍaśacā pūrva pañcadhā ca dvidhā punaḥ
padasyāṃśo'paraḥ pūrvo dvātriṃśadamāpnuyāt
tāntrikāṃśca tathā''kārānupajīvanti kecana
yathā vā śaktimīśasya yathā vā bhūtapañcakam
tathā sarve padākārānupajīvanti sarvadā
mātṛkā paramā devī svapadākārameditā
vaikharīrūpatāmeti karaṇairviśadā svayam
sthūlā sūkṣmā susūkṣmā ca trividhā mātṛkeśvarī
sā devī śaktisaṃbhinnā śivasyāmitatejasaḥ
vācāmagocarākāro mātṛkāyāstathā paraḥ
brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāmacintyaḥ sūkṣmatāvidhiḥ
cinmayaḥ paracidrūpaḥ śivāsaṃbhinna eva hi
ācāryamukhataḥ prāṃjñāḥ sidhyatyevācireṇa tu
ācāryarahito mantraḥ puṃso'narthasya kāraṇam
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sutasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
nāma caturtho'dhyāyaḥ
atha pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ
praṇavaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāva
paraḥ parataraṃ brahma prajñānandādilakṣaṇam
prakarṣeṇa navaṃ yasmātparaṃ brahma svabhāvataḥ
aparaḥ praṇavaḥ sākṣācchabdarūpaḥ sunirmalaḥ
prakarṣeṇa navatvasya hetutvātpraṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ
purā prajāpatiḥ sākṣācchraddhayā parayā saha
bhasmoddhūlitasarvāṅgastripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakaḥ
sadā pañcāgnimadhyasthaḥ sāmbadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
sa punaḥ śaṃkarasyāsya prasādādamvikāpateḥ
pṛthivīmantarikṣaṃ ca divaṃ cāsṛjadāstikāḥ
sa tānabhyatapallokāṃstebhyo vedavidāṃ varāḥ
trīṇi jyotīṃṣyajāyanta pṛthivyā eva tatra tu
ajāyatāgnirvāyuśca brāhmaṇāśvānterikṣataḥ
divo divākaraḥ sākṣājagaccakṣurajāyata
tāni cābhyatapajyotīṃṣyajastebhyo mahādvijāḥ
trayo vedā ajāyanta vedānāṃ prathamo'nalāva
yajurvedastathā vāyorādityātsāmasaṃjñitaḥ
vedānabhyatapattāṃśca brahmā tebhyo mahādijāḥ
trīṇi śuklānyajāyanta tatra brahmavidāṃ varāḥ
ajāyanta krameṇaiva koṭisūryasamaprabhāḥ
akāraśca tathokāro makāraśceti suvratāḥ
sarvāvabhāsako nityamabhavatpaṇḍitottamāḥ
jñātārthe jñātamityevaṃ vaktavye sati tahinā
omiti prāha loko'yaṃ tena jñātasya vācakaḥ
ajñātārthe tathā'jñātamiti prāpte tu vācake
omiti prāha loko'yaṃ tenājñātasya vācakaḥ
ākāśādipadārthānāṃ ye śabdā vācakā bhuvi
vinā tānakhilā śabdāloka omiti bhāṣate
ataḥ prayogavāhulyāṭakuyyādiśabdavat
ākāśādipadārthānāṃ vācakaḥ praṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ
sarvāvabhāsakatvena brahmaṇā sadṛśaḥ smṛtaḥ
paramātmābhivaḥ śaṃbhurdevatā parikīrtitā
akāro bindusaṃyuktaḥ śaktirasya dvijottamāḥ
ukāraśca makāraśca dvayaṃ bījaṃ prakīrtitam
agniśva vāyuḥ sūryaśva varṇānāṃ munayaḥ kramāt
gāyatrī ca tathā triṣṭubbṛhatī ca yathākramam
chandāṃsi brahmavicchreṣṭhā varṇānāṃ ca yathākramam
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśva varṇānāṃ devatāḥ kramāt
raktaṃ śuktaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca kramāddarṇā udāhṛtāḥ
jāgratsvamasuṣuptiśvāvasthāḥ proktā yathākramam
bhūmyantarikṣasvargāśca sthānāni kramaśo viduḥ
udāttapramukhā viprāḥ svarāḥ proktā manīpibhiḥ
ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñāśca vedāḥ proktā yathākramam
proktaścā''havanīyāgnirvarṇānāṃ kramaśo dvijāḥ
prātarmadhyaṃdinaṃ sāyaṃ kālā uktā yathākramam
rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamaścaiva guṇā uktā yathākramam
sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśva saṃhāraḥ kriyāḥ proktā yathākramam
utpattau ca sthitau nāśe viniyogā udāhṛtāḥ
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntamaṅgulīnāṃ ca saṃdhiṣu
aṅgulīṣu ca sarvāsu praṇavanyāsa īritaḥ
hṛdayādipradeśeṣu krameṇaiva dvijottamāḥ
japenmantravaraṃ bhaktyā lakṣāṇāṃ daśakaṃ dvijāḥ
ṣaṭkarmāṇi prasidhyanti tathaivāṣṭa vibhūtayaḥ
sarvavidyālayo bhūtvā yatheṣṭaṃ phalamāpnuyāt
vicāro nāma pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ
nāma pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ
sāvitrīmatha vakṣyāmi vyāhṛtyā śirasā saha
bhūrādivyāhṛtīnāṃ tu munayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
kaśyapaśvāṅgirāśveti krameṇa munipuṅgavāḥ
vyāhṛtīnāṃ krameṇaiva chandāṃsi kathitāni tu
devīgāyatramādyaṃ syāduṣṇihā tadanantaram
anuṣṭubbṛhatī paṅaktistriṣṭup ca jagatī tathā
agnirvāyustathā'rkaśva vāgīśo varuṇastathā
indraśva viśvedevāśca krameṇaiva tu devatāḥ
vyāhṛtīnāṃ tu sarvatra viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
viśvāmitro muniśchando gāyatraṃ devatā raviḥ
sāvitryā vedavicchreṣṭhāḥ śiva evādhidevatā
tripadā sā tu sāvitrī ṣaḍbhirvarṇaiścatuṣpadā
jape sā tripadā jñeyā pūjāyāṃ sā catuṣpadā
ṛṣirbrahmā'sya mantrasya cchando'nuṣṭup prakīrtitaḥ
yatheṣṭasādhane cāsya viniyoga udāhṛtaḥ
sāvitrī tripadā jñeyā paṭṭūkṣiḥ pañcaśīrṣakā
agnivarṇamukhā śuklā puṇḍarīkadalekṣaṇā
ṛgyajuḥsāmarūpāśca pādā asyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
pūrvā dikprathamā kukṣirdvitīyā dakṣiṇā matā
paścimā diktṛtīyā ca caturthī cottarā matā
ūrdhvā dikpañcamī kukṣiḥ ṣaṣṭhayadho dikprakīrtitā
aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni nābhirasyā munīśvarāḥ
jagaccharīraṃ sāvitryā jākāśamudarāntaram
stanau chandāṃsi hṛdayaṃ dharmaśāstramakalmaṣam
bāhavo nyāyaśāstraṃ tu karṇau sāṃkhyadayaṃ tathā
śikṣādyaṅgāni śīrṣāṇi vaktramagnirmahādyutiḥ
mīmāṃsā lakṣaṇaṃ tasyāśveśa cā''tharvaṇī śrutiḥ
brahmā mūrdhā śikhā rudro viṣṇurātmā prakīrtitaḥ
tasyāḥ sūkṣmaśarīraṃ ca śāstraṃ vedāntasaṃjñitam
antaryāmī śivaḥ sākṣātsāmbaścandrārdhaśekharaḥ
svaśarīre tu sāvitrīṃ vinyasedakṣarakramāt
pādāṅguṣṭhe tu gulphe tu jaṅghe jānupradeśake
kaṇṭhe ca vadane tālau nāsikāyāṃ ca cakṣupoḥ
dakṣiṇa paścime caiva tathaiva brāhmaṇottamāḥ
prathamaśvampakākāro dvitīyaḥ śyāma eva hi
tṛtīyaḥ piṅgalaḥ moktaścaturtho munisattamāḥ
vidyuddarṇanibhaḥ sākṣādaṣṭamaḥ paribhāṣitaḥ
navamastārakāvarṇo daśamaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇakaḥ
tatparo raktagaurābhaḥ śyāmastatparamaḥ smṛtaḥ
śuklavarṇaḥ pītavarṇo raktavarṇaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ
śuklavarṇaḥ paro varṇaḥ padmarāgaprabhaḥ paraḥ
tatparaḥ śaśisaṃkāśaḥ pāṇḍuraḥ paramo mataḥ
goraktasadṛśaśvānyastatparaḥ sūryasaṃnibhaḥ
śaṅkhakundenduvarṇābhaḥ sākṣāddarṇaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ
tatparo dīpasaṃkāśaḥ kramādvarṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
keciddarṇāstu sāvitryā mahāpātakanāśanāḥ
upapātakapāpānāṃ varṇāḥ kecana bādhakāḥ
kecana kṣudrapāpānāṃ nāśakāḥ syurna saṃśayaḥ
nānatoyasamaṃ dānaṃ na cāhiṃsāparaṃ tapaḥ
na sāvitrīsamaṃ japyaṃ na vyāhṛtisamaṃ hutam
yo no'smākaṃ dhiyaścittānyantaryāmisvarūpataḥ
savituḥ svātmabhūtaṃ tu vareṇyaṃ sarvajantubhiḥ
tacchabdavācyaṃ sarvajñaṃ jagatsargādikāraṇam
svamāyāśaktisaṃbhinnaṃ śivarudrādisaṃjñitam
nīlagrīvaṃ virūpākṣaṃ sāmvamūrtyapalakṣitam
ādityenāparijñātaṃ vayaṃ dhīmahyupāsmahe
sāvitryāḥ kathito hyarthaḥ saṃgraheṇa mayā''dāt
caturviṃśatikaṃ lakṣaṃ japedavyagrataḥ sudhīḥ
ājyena juhuyānmantrī sahasrāṇāṃ catuṣṭayam
srātvā prātarjapennityaṃ sahasraṃ śraddhayā saha
apekṣitārtha sakalaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
hutvā tu khādiraṃ samyagvṛtāktaṃ havyavāhane
rāhusūryasamāvāye tarpayedbhāskaraṃ jalaiḥ
sarvakāmasamṛddhiḥ syānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā
karīpacūrṇato hutvā sarpipā saha mānavaḥ
gavāṃ goṣṭhe sahasraṃ tu bahukṣirāṃ labheta gām
śālyāstaṇḍulahomena kanyāsiddhirbhaviṣyati
śolībījasya homena prajāmiṣṭāmavāpnuyāt
sāvitryā jalamādāya jatvā cāṣṭasahasrakam
abhiṣekaṃ dvijaḥ kuryādduḥsvaprādinivṛttaye
śrīharī japeearttyuvināśane
ghṛtāhāro japeddidyāṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
nābhimātre jale sthitvā japellakṣaṃ samāhitaḥ
akaṇṭakaṃ mahārājyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
palāśapuṣpahomena mahatīṃ śriyamaśnute
vetasairjayādau dṛṣṭiṃ śīghramavāpnuyāt
madhuhomena viprendrā rājānaṃ vaśamāyāt
pāyasaṃ madhunā hutvā strīvaśyaṃ labhate'cirāt
kevalaṃ ghṛtahomena sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
annasya homataśvānnaṃ prāpnuyādacireṇa tu
pañcagavyāśano lakṣaṃ japtvā jātismaro bhavet
saptāhānmārayecchamṛte vipraṃ na saṃśayaḥ
śatroḥ pratikṛtiṃ bhūmāvālikhyā''khyāṃ ca tahṛdi
sāvitrī pratilomā syādabhicāreṣu karmasu
māraṇe varṇaśaḥ śatrorbrahmāstraṃ pratilomataḥ
śāntaye juhuyādanau ghṛtena payasā'pi vā
pañcagavyena vā hutvā tilairvā śāntimāpnuyāt
udumbarabhavāśvatthaigegajāśvāmayakṣayaḥ
payasā''jyena vā hutvā śāntiḥ sarvacatuṣpadām
śāntaye sarvadoṣāṇāṃ jānumātre jale japet
abhimantrya sitaṃ bhasma nyaseḍūtādiśāntaye
vahunoktena kiṃ viprā japenāsyāśva homataḥ
abhīṣṭaṃ sarvamāproti nātra saṃdehakāraṇam
jñānecchāṃ tatprasādena labhate ca dvijottamāḥ
sāvitrījapayajñena jñānayajñamavāpnuyāt
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
khaṇḍe gāyatrīvivaraṇaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ
nāma ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣirbrahmā'sya gāyatraṃ chanda ātmaiva devatā
śāntāntaṃ śaktirasyoktā tadantaṃ bījamucyate
vidyā śaktirbhavedvījaṃ śiva eva na cānyathā
tenāyaṃ paramo mantraḥ śivaśaktyātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ
etadbuddhvā japenmantraṃ bījaśakyātmanā budhaḥ
dhyāyetsāmyaṃ mahādevaṃ saṃsārāmayabheṣajam
yastu dvādaśasāhasramimaṃ japati nityaśaḥ
tasya sarvāṇi pāpāni vinaśyanti na saṃśayaḥ
athavā prāṇasaṃcāraḥ sakāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ
hakāro'pānasaṃcāro dehe dehabhṛtāṃ sadā
evaṃ yastu vijānāti mantramācāryapūrvakam
so'japannapi haṃsākhyaṃ japatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
īdṛśīmajapāṃ vidyāmāstikyādgurubhaktitaḥ
yo vijānāti pāpāni buddhipūrvakṛtāni ca
tasya naśyanti sarvāṇi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
athavo jīvamantro'yaṃ jīvātmapratipādakaḥ
ahaṃśabdasya rūḍhatvāloke jīvātmavastuni
śaktimantraḥ sakārākhyaḥ parameśvaravācakaḥ
saṃsāritvena bhāto'haṃ sa eva parameśvaraḥ
so'hameva na saṃdehaḥ svānubhūtipramāṇataḥ
haṃsayoḥ śabalaṃ hitvā padayoḥ sadditīyayoḥ
pūrṇo'hamevaṃ jānīyādbodhamātrasvabhāvataḥ
śrutirapyevamevā''ha paramārthaprakāśinī
satyasaṃpūrṇa vijñāna sukharūpo maheśvaraḥ
ahaṃ cāvyabhicāritvātsatsvabhāvo na saṃśayaḥ
ahamavyabhicāryeva sākṣitvādvyabhicāriṇām
jñātamajñātamapyarthaṃ sadā'haṃ veda kevalaḥ
śarāvādipadārthānāṃ cetanatvaprasaktitaḥ
tathā cicetanasyāpi na śeṣatvamavāpnuyāt
ato'nyaśeṣatā loke cito bhrāntyā pratīyate
sukhasvabhāva evāhaṃ sadā premāspadatvataḥ
nāhamanyasya śeṣo hi śeṣī sarvasya sarvadā
pūrṇo'haṃ sarvasākṣitvātsarvadā paramārthataḥ
apūrṇo yugapatsarvaṃ na vijānāti kaścana
saṃsāravarjitaḥ sākṣātsarvadā parameśvaraḥ
ahaṃ saṃsārasākṣitvāttathā saṃsāravarjitaḥ
evaṃ vākyānusāriṇyā yuktyā''cāryapuraḥsaram
ahaṃ sa so'hameveti vijānīyādvicakṣaṇaḥ
ya evamātmamantreṇa jīvātmaparamātmanoḥ
pāramārthikamekatvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ paripaśyati
evaṃbhūtaṃ parijñānaṃ yasya jātaṃ yadā bhuvi
tadaiva tasya saṃsāravināśo nāsti saṃśayaḥ
haṃsavidyāmavijñāya muktau yatnaṃ karoti yaḥ
haṃsavidyā parā caiṣā paramantraprabhedinī
sarvaiśvaryapradā sarvadevatā tṛptikāriṇī
asyāśca japamātreṇa dīrghāyuṣyamavāpnuyāt
ārogyaṃ vijayaṃ vidyāmavāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ
bahunoktena kiṃ vidyā haṃsākhyā sarvakāmadā
haṃsa haṃseti yo brūyātsarvadā śiva eva saḥ
śivena viṣṇunā caiva brahmaṇā sarvadaivataiḥ
nābhikande samau kṛtvā prāṇāpānau samāhitaḥ
mastakasthāmṛtasvādaṃ pītvā dhyānena sādaram
dīpākāraṃ mahādevaṃ jvalantaṃ nābhimadhyame
īśvaratvamavāproti sadā'bhyāsaparaḥ pumān
bahavo'nena mārgeṇa prāptā nityatvamāstikāḥ
yo dadāti mahāvidyāṃ haṃsākhyāṃ parameśvarīm
tasya dāsyaṃ sadā kuryācchūddhayā parayā saha
śubhaṃ vā'śubhamanyadvā yaduktaṃ guruṇā bhuvi
tatkuryādavicāreṇa śiṣyaḥ saṃtoṣasaṃyuktaḥ
haṃsavidyāmimāṃ labdhvā guroḥ śuśrūṣayā naraḥ
ātmānamātmanā sākṣādbrahma buddhvā suniścalaḥ
dehajātyādisaṃbandhānvarṇāśramasamanvitān
vedāśāstrāṇi cānyāni pādapāṃsumiva tyajet
na guruṃ saṃtyajennityaṃ jānannasya kṛtaṃ naraḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
khaṇḍe haṃsavidyāvivaraṇaṃ nāma saptamo'dhyāyaḥ
nāma saptamo'dhyāyaḥ
paḍakṣaraṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsena suśobhanam
devatā'sya śivaḥ sākṣātsatyajñānasukhādayaḥ
śaktirmāheśvarī sā ca bhuvaneśākṣaraṃ bhavet
vījaṃ māyāviśiṣṭastu śivaḥ pūrvoktalakṣaṇaḥ
so'pi tacchabda eva syānnyāsaḥ pañcākṣaraiḥ kramāt
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ vinyasedakṣaraṃ kramāt
punaḥ pañcākṣareṇaiva pañcāṅgaṃ visanyetkramāt
praṇavaṃ prathamaṃ vidyādditīyaṃ tu nakārakam
makāraṃ tatparaṃ vidyācchikāraṃ tu tataḥ param
vakāraṃ pañcamaṃ vidyādyakāraṃ paṣṭhameva ca
itthaṃ paḍakṣaraṃ vidyājjābālopaniṣadgatam
asaṃpṛktyā śivasyāyaṃ śivaśabdastu vācakaḥ
namaḥ śabdo namaskāravācakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
prahṛtālakṣaṇaḥ prokto namaskāraḥ purātanaiḥ
prahnatā nāma jīvasya śivātsatyādilakṣaṇāt
bhedena bhāsamānasya māyayā na svarūpataḥ
saṃbandha eva tenaiva so'pi tādātmyalakṣaṇaḥ
nityasiddha ḥ śivaḥ sākṣātsvarūpaḥ sarvadehinām
tasmādubhutsorjīvasya nopādeyaṃ hitaṃ sadā
evaṃ vidyānnakārārthaṃ makārārtha udīryate
vyāvahārikadṛṣṭyā'yaṃ namaskāraḥ prakīryate
joṅkāraśabdaḥ sarvārthavācakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
tasmācchivasya pūrṇasya praṇavo vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvaśva lakṣyalakṣaṇatā'pi ca
asti nāsti mṛpā bhāti na bhātītyādi māyayā
māyātatkāryamapyasmācchivātsatyādilakṣaṇāva
śivasvarūpamevā''huridaṃ sarva vicakṣaṇāḥ
sarvasvarūpamajñānādṛśyate na tu vastutaḥ
vedāḥ sarve purāṇāni smṛtayo bhārataṃ tathā
anyānyapi ca śāstrāṇi tathā tarkāśva sarvaśaḥ
śaivāgamāśca vividhā āgamā vaiṣṇavā api
anyāgamāśca viduṣāmanubhūtistathaiva ca
bādhyabādhakatāṃ yānti vyavahāre parasparam
ācāryamukhato mantraṃ jñātvā sāthai samāhitaḥ
srānaṃ triṣavaṇaṃ kṛtvā bhasmanā śākabhojanaḥ
phalamūlāśano vā'pi haviṣyāśī yathāvalam
parvatāgre nadītīre sāgarānte śivālaye
samāhitamanā bhūtvā sukhamāsanamāsthitaḥ
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā muniṃ chandastathaiva ca
devatāṃ caṃ tathā śaktiṃ vījaṃ smṛtvā manorapi
karanyāsaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā tathā'ṅganyāsameva ca
hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhye tu somasūryāgnimaṇḍale
śivaṃ dhyātvā japenmantraṃ lakṣāṇāṃ pad samāhitaḥ
ājyena payasā vā'pi palāśakusumena vā
athavā sāmvamīśānaṃ śrīsadāśivameva ca
nṛtyamānaṃ tathā deveṃ dhyātvā mantraṃ tu sādhayet
athavā prākṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ svīyamutsṛjya sarvadā
nityaṃ dvādaśasāhasraṃ japeddhatayā samāhitaḥ
samyagjñānapṭhavaṃ labdhvā saṃsārābdhi tariṣyati
lakṣapañcāśataṃ japtvā kāraṇeśvaramāpnuyāt
lakṣāṇāṃ tu śataṃ japtvā sākṣādrudratvamāpnuyāt
aśītilakṣaṃ japtvā tu naro viṣṇutvamāpnuyāt
catvāriṃśatibhirlakṣairvirāḍātmānamāpnuyāt
viṃśalakṣajapenaiva dīrghamāyuravāśayāt
viniyogaḥ samākhyātaḥ pūjā devasya kīrtyate
hṛtpadmakarṇikāmadhye mantreṇānena pūjayet
athavā maṇḍale saure candramaṇḍalake'thavā
agnau vā pratimāyāṃ vā śivaṃ nityaṃ prapūjayeva
āsanaṃ prathamaṃ dadyādāvāhanamanantaram
arghyaṃ tataḥ paraṃ dadyātpādyaṃ caiva tataḥ param
vāso dadyātpunaryajñopavītaṃ bhūpaṇāni ca
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ dīpamodanameva ca
paḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa sarvaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ
hṛtpadmakarṇikāmadhyātkuryādāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ
udāsanaṃ ca tatraiva naraḥ kuryātsamāhitaḥ
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena narāṇāṃ bhuktimuktaye
paḍakṣareṇa sarvāṇi sidhyantyeva na saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
khaṇḍe paḍakṣaravivaraṇaṃ nāmāṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ
varaṇaṃ nāmāṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ
dhyānayajñamathedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ
śṛṇuta śraddhayā yūyaṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam
na svarūpeṇa sākṣitvādātmatvādviṣayitvataḥ
umārdhavigrahā śuklā candrārdhakṛtaśekharā
nīlagrīvā trinetrā ca prasannavadanā śubhā
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā
svasvarūpānusaṃdhānapramodādeva kevalāva
mahātāṇḍavasaṃyuktā brahmaviṣṇuśivādibhiḥ
dhyeyā''dyantavinirmuktā yā mūrtiḥ śrutidarśitā
saivāsādhāraṇā mūrtiḥ parātparatarasya tu
ye sadā paramāṃ mūrti dhyāyanti hṛdayāmbuje
imāṃ te paramāṃ muktiṃ muktiṃ ca prāpnuvanti hi
jñānājñānamahāmāyālakṣaṇāvidyayā saha
samapradhānarūpeṇāpyādareṇa manīṣibhiḥ
jāḍyākārastu yaḥ śaktestenābhinnaṃ paraṃ padam
svapradhānādirūpeṇa tridhopāsyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ
tathā śaktestu yo jñānākārastenaikatāṃ gatam
paratattvaṃ tridhopāsyaṃ parijñānavatāṃ varāḥ
māyākāraikatāpannamapi tattvaṃ manīṣibhiḥ
anye ca śakterākārā ye vidyante vicakṣaṇāḥ
upāsyaṃ trividhaṃ nityamatīva śraddhayā saha
īkṣaṇopādhisaṃpannaṃ paratattvamapi dvijāḥ
svapradhānādirūpeṇa tridhopāsyamatipriyāt
sattvaṃ rajastamaśveti guṇā ye brahmaśaktijāḥ
te jagannāśasargādeḥ kartāraḥ kāryarūpiṇaḥ
upāsyāstrividhā nityaṃ te'pi svaṃ svamupādhibhiḥ
tairgṛhītāstathā viprā mūrtayastriprakārataḥ
cittapākānuguṇyena cintanīyā manīṣibhiḥ
śabdasparśādisaṃjñā ye padārthāḥ pañca te'pi ca
upāsyā brahmarūpeṇa mahāprājñairmanīpibhiḥ
ākāśādīni bhūtāni yāni tāni manīṣibhiḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāni mahātmabhiḥ
bhautikā aṇḍabhedāśva brahmarūpeṇa sādaram
cintanīyāśca vidyadbhirvedavedāntapāragāḥ
aṇḍamadhye sthitā lokā ete'pi brahmavittamāḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā eva sūribhiḥ
lokāntarvartino deśā ete'pi dijapuṅgavāḥ
merumandārapūrvāśca parvatā vividhā dvijāḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā vedavittamāḥ
nadīnadādayaḥ sarve devarṇyādivinirmitāḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāḥ puruṣottamaiḥ
vāpīkūpataḍāgādyā api vedaparāyaṇāḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāḥ puruṣādhikaiḥ
samudrāśva sadā viprāḥ samudrāntargatā api
diśaśva vidiśaścaiva divārātraṃ tathaiva ca
anāgatādayaḥ kālā upāsyā brahmarūpataḥ
aṇḍajaṃ jārajaṃ caiva svedajaṃ codvijaṃ tathā
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā api ca saṃkarāḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā eva sūribhiḥ
āśramā brahmacaryādyāstadācārā api dvijāḥ
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāḥ paramāstikaiḥ
mahāpātakapūrvāṇi pāpāni subahūni ca
dharmasaṃjñāśca ye viprā uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ
te'pi brahmatayā nityamupāsyāḥ paṇḍitottamaiḥ
sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ tayorbhogaḥ sādhanaṃ tasya suvratāḥ
brahmarūpatayā sarvamupāsyaṃ satyavādibhiḥ
kartā kārayitā karma karaṇaṃ kāryameva ca
pramātā ca pramāṇaṃ ca prameyaṃ pramitistathā
brahmarūpatayā sarvamupāsyaṃ mānamānibhiḥ
avandhyāśca tathā vandhyā vādāśca vividhā api
brahmarūpatayā sarvamupāsyaṃ vākyavedibhiḥ
sa yāti dhyānayajñena sākṣāddijñānamaiśvaram
dhyānayajñasya māhātmyaṃ kalpānāṃ koṭikoṭibhiḥ
dhyānayajñaṃ vinā muktau yatante mohitā janāḥ
pāyasānnaṃ parityajya bhakṣayanti mahāviṣam
dhyānayajñaṃ vinā kiṃcitkurvāṇo muktisiddhayeṃ
akṣṇā'pi śabdaṃ gṛhṇāti vinā śrotreṇa kevalam
aśvamedhādayo yajñā aśeṣā vedadarśitāḥ
munīndrā dhyānayajñasya kalāṃ nārhanti poḍaśīm
dhyānayajñaparo maryaḥ śiva eva na cāparaḥ
dhyānayajñaparāṇāṃ tu prasādaṃ kurute śivaḥ
śivo'pi sākṣātsarvajñaḥ saṃsāravinivartakaḥ
kurudhvaṃ vedavinmukhyā dhyānayajñamaśaṅkitāḥ
yajñavivaraṇa nāma navamo'dhyāyaḥ
dhyānayajñavivaraṇaṃ nāma navamo'dhyāyaḥ
athedānoṃ pravakṣyāmi jñānayajñasya vaibhavam
jñānayajñātparo yajño nāsti viprāḥ śrutau smṛtau
jñānaṃ bahuvidhaṃ proktaṃ vedārthajñānapāragaiḥ
svarūpamekaṃ vijñānaṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ
māyākāreṇa saṃvaddhaṃ jaḍaśakteḥ śivasya tu
jñānamīśvarasaṃjñaṃ ca niyantu jagato bhavet
śakteravidyākāreṇa saṃvaddhaṃ jīvasaṃjñitam
jīvasaṃjñaṃ tu vijñānaṃ dvidhā loke vyavasthitam
sthūlasūkṣmaśarīrābhyāmavacchinnaṃ pratītitaḥ
svapracārāśrayaṃ cittaṃ jīvarūpaprakāśakam
jñātṛtva heturjīvasya duḥkhitvādeśva kāraṇam
pramāṇabhrāntisaṃdehādyākāreṇa munīśvarāḥ
bahurūpaṃ bhavecittaṃ kālakarmavipākataḥ
tattadākārasaṃbhinnaṃ vijñānaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
pramāṇacāntisaṃdehajñānamityucyate'naghāḥ
aduṣṭakaraṇotpannaṃ vijñānaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
pramāṇajñānamityuktaṃ munibhiḥ sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ
duṣṭakāraṇavijñānaṃ bhrāntijñānaṃ pracakṣate
koṭiyāvalambi syātsaṃdehajñānamāstikāḥ
itthamevedamityevaṃrūpaṃ yatsphuraṇaṃ budhāḥ
jñānasya tena saṃvandhaḥ prāmāṇyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā
pramāṇajñānasāmagryaḥ paṇmayā'bhihitā budhāḥ
tatraikā'bhāvavijñānasāmagrī kathitā dvijāḥ
anyā tu bhāvavijñānasāmagrī parikīrtitā
yadyogyānupalabdhyaiva janyaṃ vijñānamāstikāḥ
tatsyādabhāvavijñānaṃ dhārmikā vedavittamāḥ
indriyotpannavijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ paribhāṣitam
vyāptijanyaparijñānamanumānamitīṣyate
sādṛśyahetujaṃ jñānamupamānamudāhṛtam
tātpayoṃpetaśabdotthajñānaṃ śābdamudāhṛtam
akṣarāṇi tathā viprāḥ padāni ca tathaiva ca
vākyāni ceti tatrāpi keṣāṃcidra dvijapuṅgavāḥ
arthānāmakṣarāṇyeva vācakāni tathaiva ca
arthānāmapi keṣāṃcitpadānyeva dvijottamāḥ
vācakāni ca vākyāni tathaiva brahmavittamāḥ
arthānāmapi keṣāṃcitpramāṇāni pradīpavat
bhavantyekākṣarāṇyeva padāni dijapuṅgavāḥ
akṣarāṇi ca saṃbhūya padāni syustathaiva ca
padānāṃ samudāyastu bhaveddākyaṃ dvijottamāḥ
pradhānaṃ guṇabhūtaṃ ca dvividhaṃ vākyamīritam
mahāvākyamiti proktaṃ pradhānaṃ munipuṅgavaiḥ
guṇabhṛtaṃ tu yadvākyaṃ tadvāntarasaṃjñitam
padāni śaktyā svārthānāṃ vācakāni tathaiva ca
tātparyādeva vākyāni svārthānāṃ bodhakāni ca
tātparye tu dvidhā viprāḥ proktaṃ vākyaviśāradaiḥ
tatraivaṃ sati vākyāni kānicitpaṇḍitottamāḥ
niṣedharūpāṇyeva syustathā viprāstu kānicit
vidhirūpāṇi cānyāni kānici dvijapuṅgavāḥ
siddhārthabodhakānyeva tatraivaṃ sati vāḍavāḥ
siddhārthabodhakaṃ vākyaṃ laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ tu vā
dviprakāramiti proktaṃ munibhiḥ sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ
prāptaprāptiparaṃ caikamaparaṃ paṇḍitottamāḥ
pratyakṣādipramāṇāni pañca ca brāhmaṇottamāḥ
kartavyaviṣayaṃ vākyamanātmaviṣayāṇi tu
parāgarthaikaniṣṭhatvātmatyaktvādātmavastunaḥ
pratyagbhūtaḥ śivo jñātuṃ na śakyaḥ sarvajantubhiḥ
sarvāntaraḥ antaḥ praviṣṭaḥ śāstā janānā sarvātmā iti ca śruteḥ
pratyagātmā śivaḥ sākṣāna parāgartha āstikāḥ
sidvārthavodhakaṃ vākyaṃ laukikaṃ kiṃcidāstikāḥ
anātmaviṣayaṃ tena śivo jñātuṃ na śakyate
kiṃcitsiddhārthakaṃ vākyaṃ laukikaṃ śrutipūrvakam
pratyagrūpe śive sākṣātpramāṇaṃ bhavati dvijāḥ
vedāntānāṃ mahāvākyaṃ pratyagbrahmakatārthagam
bhūmānanda śivaprāptisādhanaṃ parikīrtitam
ātmā svabhāvato baddho yadi syādvedavittamāḥ
dharmiṇā saha tannāśo bhavatyeva na cānyathā
ātmano naiva nāśo'sti kadācidapi suvratāḥ
yato ghaṭādernāśastu dṛṣṭo viprā anātmanaḥ
ghaṭādyupādhisaṃparkādākāśasya bhidā yathā
āhuścidrūpato bhedaśvito nāstyeva sarvathā
ātmabhūtaḥ śivaḥ sākṣāñcinmātrajyotireva hi
vaṭādīnāṃ tu caityānāmanātmatvasya darśanāva
mātmano'pi khato bhedamāhuḥ kecinmunīśvarāḥ
tanna saṃgatameva syādātmā bhedasya sādhakaḥ
bhedasākṣī śivo hyātmā kathaṃ bhinno bhaveddijāḥ
aṅgīkṛtya ghaṭādīnāṃ bhedaṃ vedārthapāragāḥ
nirastaśvā''tmabhedastu ghaṭādīnāṃ bhidā'pi ca
bhrāntisiddhā na satyoktā tarkataśva pramāṇataḥ
ghaṭādīnāṃ bhidā tāvanna bhrāntaiva pratītitaḥ
pratītyā satyarūpaiva vyavahāre munīśvarāḥ
māyāmātramidaṃ dvaitamiti cā''ha parā śrutiḥ
ekatvaṃ paśyato mohaḥ kaḥ śoka iti cā''ha hi
atastarkapramāṇābhyāṃ vastvekatvaṃ suniśvitam
viduṣāmanubhūtyā ca vastvekatvaṃ suniśvitam
vastvekatvaṃ mahāvākyādeva jānanti ye janāḥ
bhedadarśanamāsthāya muktiṃ vāñchanti ye narāḥ
te mahāghorasaṃsāre patantyeva na saṃśayaḥ
sarvabhūteṣu cā''tmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cā''tmani
saṃpaśyannātmayājī syātsvārājyamadhigacchati
sarvabhūtāni saṃpaśyatrātmanyeva munīśvarāḥ
saṃsārasāgarādasmāduttīrṇaḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ
dvaitavijñānamāsādya muktiṃ vāñchanti ye narāḥ
te mahāmohasaṃsārasarpadaṣṭā na saṃśayaḥ
ātmayāthātmyavijñānayajñaṃ muktvā narādhamāḥ
kriyārūpeṣu yajñeṣu yatante māyayā'nṛtāḥ

aho māheśvarajñānaṃ yajñavaibhavamāstikāḥ

śrutyā śivena vā viprā jñānayajñasya vaibhavam
jñānayajñavivaraṇaṃ nāma daśamo'dhyāyaḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
indrādidevatāstittvaṃ yeṣāṃ citte prakāśate
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
brahmā viśiṣṭo devānāmiti jānanti ye janāḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
viṣṇorviśiṣṭaṃ rudra ye vijānanti pramāṇataḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
īśvarādadhiko bhāti yeṣāṃ citte sadāśivaḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
sadāśivādapi śreṣṭhaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ye janā viduḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
viṣṇostu paramaṃ sākṣādudaṃ jānanti ye janāḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
īkṣiturye vijānanti sarvajñaṃ nitarāṃ param
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
kāraṇaṃ brahma sarveṣāṃ viśiṣṭamiti ye viduḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
kāraṇatvopalakṣyaṃ ye sarvotkṛṣṭaṃ śivaṃ viduḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
asti jīvo na nāstīti ye jānanti pramāṇataḥ
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ

te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyākhyaṃ veda dhāmatrayaṃ tu yaḥ
sa evā''tmā na taddṛśyaṃ dṛśyaṃ tasminprakalpitam
tridhāmasākṣiṇaṃ saṃtyajñānānandādilakṣaṇam
tvamahaṃśabdalakṣyārthamasaktaṃ sarvadoṣataḥ
jñātājñātadvayādanyaṃ jñātājñātasya bhāsakam
pramāṇabhrāntivṛttīnāmagamyaṃ tatprakāśakam
svayaṃbhātaṃ nirādhāraṃ ye jānanti suniścitam
te'pi vijñānasaṃpannā iti me niścitā matiḥ
uktalakṣaṇamātmānamuktalakṣaṇamīśvaram
ekaṃ paśyanti ye viprāstarkataśca pramāṇataḥ
jñānayajñaviśeṣo nāmaikādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
vakhaṇḍa ekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
bhūyo'pi jñānayajñaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ
munayaḥ parayā bhaktyā śṛṇutātīva śobhanam
brahma satyaparānandaprakāśānantalakṣaṇam
ātmaśaktisamāyogādnādyantādatarkitāva
apratītamivā''bhāti svayaṃbhātamapi dvijāḥ
tādṛśākāramāpannaḥ saṃsāravāvabhāsate
vibhāgaḥ kalpitaḥ śaktyā na svataḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ
brahmaṇaścetanākāre kalpitā cetanābhidā
utkarṣaścāpakarṣaśca māyayā tepu kalpitaḥ
niyantṛtvaniyamyatvādyākārāśca prakalpitāḥ
brahmaṇo'cetanākāre mahāmāyābalena tu
utkarṣaścāpakarṣaśca jagatyapi munīśvarāḥ
varṇāśramāstathā viprā varṇasāṃkaryameva ca
tamīśva vibhāgena māyayaiva prakalpitāḥ
varṇāśramādiniṣṭhānāṃ māyayaiva prakalpitam
vidhayaśca niṣedhāśva śrutismṛtyādirūpiṇaḥ
kalpitāni mahāmohādvahmaṇo na svabhāvataḥ
rāgadveṣādayo doṣāḥ śāntidānyādayo guṇāḥ
api māheśvaraṃ jñānaṃ māyayaiva prakalpitam
vaidikāstāntrikā mārga apabhraṃśāstathaiva ca
sarvajñatvādikā bhedāḥ stambāntā ye prakalpitāḥ
utkarṣaśvāpakarṣaśva yasteṣu parikalpitaḥ
utkarṣaśvāpakarṣaśva yo jagatyapi kalpitaḥ
varṇāśramādayo bhāvā māyayā ye prakalpitāḥ
niyojyatvādayo bhāvā māyayā ye prakalpitāḥ
vidhayaśva niṣedhāśca māyayā ye prakalpitāḥ
dharmādharmādirūpeṇa māyayā ye prakalpitāḥ
rāgadveṣādirūpāśca māyayā ye prakalpitāḥ
vaidikāstāntrikā mārgā apabhraṃśāśca ye dvijāḥ
yadyadastitayā yadyannāsti vastu munīśvarāḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe satasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
khaṇḍe paḍakṣaravivaraṇaṃ nāma dvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
svasminnāśritā māyā svaśaktiḥ
jñānayajñaviśeṣo nāma dvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
bhūyo'pi jñānayajñaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ
guhyādguhyatamaṃ sūkṣmaṃ śṛṇuta śradvayā dvijāḥ
cinmātrāśrayamāyāyāḥ śaktyākāre dvijottamāḥ
anupraviṣṭā yā saṃvinnirvikalpā svayaṃprabhā
sadākārā parānandā saṃsārocchedakāriṇī
sā śivā paramā devī śivābhinnā śivaṃkarī
jagatkāraṇamāpannaḥ śivo yo munisattamāḥ

viṣṇvāgamoditādvarmādaśeṣādāstikottamāḥ
śaivāgamodito dharmo variṣṭho naiva saṃśayaḥ
śaivāgamodito dharmo dvidhā pūrvamudīritaḥ
ūrdhvasrotodbhavādvamatsmārtā dharmā mahattarāḥ
smārtabhyaḥ śrautadharmāśca variṣṭhā munisattamāḥ
teṣāṃ śāntyādayaḥ śreṣṭhāstepāṃ bhasmāvaguṇṭhanam
sātparyadīpikāsametā yajñavaibhava khaṇḍe
rudrākṣadhāraṇaṃ cāpi śivādyākhyābhibhāṣaṇam
śivaliṅgārcanaṃ bhaktyā śivo'hamiti bhāvanā
śivajñānaikaniṣṭasya śuśrūṣā ca viśiṣyate
variṣṭhaṃ sarvadharmebhyo jñānaṃ mokṣaikasādhanam
jñānānnāsti paro dharma iti vedārthanirṇayaḥ
pūrvoditebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
jñānānebhyaḥ samāsena bhasmaikaṃ paramaṃ matam
bhasmasādhananiṣṭhānāṃ sākṣādbhasma śivābhidham
prakāśate yathā śāntyā śāntaṃ vastu parātparam
jñānasya kāraṇebhyastu śrutireva mahattarā
jñānānāṃ śaṃbhuvijñānaṃ variṣṭhaṃ netaradbhavet
vedavākyasamutpannaṃ śivajñānaṃ nirūpaṇe
samyagjñānaṃ mayā''khyātamitaravyavahārataḥ
codanālakṣaṇo dharmo dharmaḥ sākṣānnirūpaṇe
āstikyānvayamātreṇa dharmābhāse'pi suvratāḥ
yathā śaṃbhumo devo nāsti puṇyavatāṃ varāḥ
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
yathā viprasamo martyo nāsti vedavidāṃ varāḥ
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
yathaivānnasamaṃ bhojyaṃ nāsti loke vicakṣaṇāḥ
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
yathā gaṅgāsamā puṇyā nadī loke na vidyate
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
yathā vārāṇasītulyā purī loke na vidyate
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
yathā gurusamatrātā nāsti saṃsārasāgarāt
tathā vedasamaṃ mānaṃ nāsti tatra na saṃśayaḥ
evamuktvā munīndrebhyaḥ śrīmānbarhiṇavāhanaḥ
kāvaṣeyā api śreṣṭhāḥ prasādāttārakāriṇaḥ
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ dadṛśuḥ svayamāgatam
taṃ praṇamya mahādevaṃ sarvajñamaparājitam
śrīmatpañcākṣareṇaiva pūjayāmāsurādarāva
devadevo mahādevo devānāmapi deśikaḥ
munibhyaḥ kāvapeyebhyaḥ svātmajñānaṃ dadau mudā
munīndrā api te sarve viśuddhajñānināṃ varāḥ
praṇamya devamīśānaṃ sāmvaṃ saṃsārabhepajam
prasādayitvā deveśaṃ kṛtārthā ātmavedanāva
dṛthā na lābhāya viśudvacetasām
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ viśiṣṭadharmavicāro
nāma viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
cāro nāma viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi muktisādhanamāstikāḥ
śṛṇuta śraddhayā sārdhaṃ sākṣāddedāntadarśitam
purā śvetādiṛpyantā munayo munisattamāḥ
saṃkhyā ca śatameteṣāṃ saha dvādaśasaṃkhyayā
ta ete bhasmadigdhāṅgāstripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakāḥ
rudrākṣamālābharaṇā rudrārādhanatatparāḥ
tapaśverurmahātīvraṃ parayā śraddhayā saha
śrīmaddakṣiṇa kailāse sākṣātsaṃsāranāśake
yasya darśanamātreṇa pāpāni sakalāni tu
dadāti paramāṃ muktimacireṇa dvijottamāḥ
yatra pratidinaṃ puṃsāṃ bhaktānāmīśvarasya tu
muṣṭimātrapradānena mahāpāpādvimucyate
brāhmaṇānāṃ tathā'nyeṣāmanantaṃ bhavati dhruvam
tapasā śaṃkarasteṣāṃ prasannaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sāmvamīśānaṃ sākṣātsaṃsārameṣajam
vakṣyāmi paramaṃ guhyaṃ muktisādhanamādāt
varṇāśramasamācārādeva muktirna cānyataḥ
sa jāyate kule mukhye viprāṇāmīśvarājñayā
sa punarjātakarmādisaṃskārairapi saṃskṛtaḥ
dārānāhṛtya yajñaṃ ca dānaṃ ca vividhaṃ tathā
tapaśva vividhaṃ ghoraṃ kṛtvā kāmanayā vinā
pranaṣṭapāpaḥ śudvāntaḥkaraṇo jñānavāñchayā
viraktaḥ sarvalokebhyo doṣāṇāṃ tu nirūpaṇāt
cittapākānuguṇyena pravrajyāṃ kurute punaḥ
tatrāmumukṣuḥ saṃnyāsī preritaḥ parameśvarāt
kuṭīcakābhiyāṃ vṛttiṃ vṛttiṃ vā'tha bahūdakām
haṃsavṛttiṃ tu vā nityaṃ vāñchate munisattamāḥ
mumukṣurbhikṣuko nityaṃ parahaṃsābhidhāṃ śubhām
kuṭīcakādivṛttistho muktimicchati ceddijāḥ
parahaṃsābhidhāṃ vṛttiṃ prāpnuyācchaṃkarājñayā
sarveṣāmeva bhikṣūṇāṃ śāntirdāntistitikṣutā
srānaṃ śaucamahiṃsā ca mithyābhāṣaṇavarjanam
tripuṇḍradhāraṇaṃ sākṣādbrahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam
line śivārcanaṃ niyaṃ dharmaḥ proktaḥ sanātanaiḥ
sākṣāddedāntavākyānāṃ śravaṇaṃ mananaṃ tathā
parahaṃsasya dharmo'yaṃ viśeṣeṇa samīritaḥ
pūrvapuṇyavalātsākṣātprasādācca śivasya tu
brahmātmaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ labhate bhikṣuko'cirāt
jñānāddedāntavākyotthānmuktiṃ bhikṣuravāpnuyāt
muktisādhanamākhyātaṃ saṃgraheṇa munīśvarāḥ
jñāne yūyamapi śraddhāṃ kurudhvaṃ yatnataḥ sadā
ityuktvā bhagavānsdraḥ sākṣātsaṃsāramocakaḥ
śrīmaddakṣiṇakailāsaṃ sarvasthānottamottamam
vāñchitārthapradaṃ nṛṇāmiti vitta vicakṣaṇāḥ
śrīmaddakṣiṇakelāsamadṛṣṭvā muktimicchataḥ
nāsti saṃsāravicchittiḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
varṇāśramasamācāraṃ vinā kaivalyamicchataḥ
nāsti kaivalyasaṃsiddhiḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
viṣṇuprajāpatīndrebhyaḥ śivasyā''dhikyamādarāt
avijñāya na saṃsārānmucyate janmakoṭibhiḥ
nāsti kaivalyamityeṣā śāśvatī śrutirāha hi
bhagavānapi sarvajñaḥ śivaḥ kāruṇikottamaḥ
vinā vedāntavijñānaṃ na muktiriti cā''ha hi
viṣṇuprajāpatīndrādidevatāśca tathaiva ca
vinā jñānaṃ na kaivalyamityāhurvedā vettamāḥ
munayaśva mahātmāmaḥ satyasaṃdhā jitendriyāḥ
vinā jñānaṃ na kaivalyamityāhurvedavittamāḥ
muktisādhanavijñānaṃ vedādeva na cānyataḥ
anyamārgajanitaṃ vicārato vedamārgarucikāraṇaṃ kramāt
muktisādhanavicāro nāmaikaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
yajñavaibhava khaṇḍe muktisādhanavicāro nāmaikaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mārgaprāmāṇyanirṇayam
śraddhayā sahitā yūyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
vedāṃśca dharmaśāstrāṇi purāṇaṃ bhārataṃ tathā
vedāṅgānyupavedāṃśva kāmikādyāgamānapi
tathā pāśupataṃ somaṃ bhairavapramukhāgamān
teṣāmevopabhedāṃśca śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ
viṣṇvāgamāṃstathā brāhmānbudvādyāgamānapi
lokāyataṃ tarkaśāstraṃ bahuvistarasaṃyutam
mīmāṃsāmatigambhīrāṃ sāṃkhyayogau tathaiva ca
anekabhedabhinnāni tathā śāstrāntarāṇi ca
nirmame śaṃkaraḥ sākṣātsarvajñaḥ saṃgraheṇa tu
prasādādeva rudrasya brahmaviṣṇvādayaḥ surāḥ
siddhavidyādharā yakṣā rākṣasādyāstathaiva ca
munayaśca manuṣyāśca yathābhāgyaṃ dvijottamāḥ
tānyeva vistareṇaiva saṃgraheṇaiva vā punaḥ
kurvanti tāni nāmāni kathitāni manīṣibhiḥ
tarkerete hi mārgāstu na hantavyā manīṣibhiḥ
yathā toyapravāhāṇāṃ samudraḥ paramāvadhiḥ
tathaiva sarvamārgāṇāṃ sākṣānniṣṭā maheśvaraḥ
tatprasādātkramānmārgānviśiṣṭāneti mānavaḥ
vedamārgasthito devaḥ sākṣānmuktestu kāraṇam
tatrāpi karmabhāgastho jñāna śraddhāprado haraḥ
jñānabhāgasthitaḥ śaṃbhujñīnadvāreṇa mokṣadaḥ
ekarūpā bhavennaiva nānārūpā bhaviṣyati
vedāntaḥ śaṃkaraṃ sākṣānnirviśepāhayātmanā
vṛkti mārgāntarānnaivaṃ tato vidyā tu vedajā
ato mārgāntarājātā matayo munisattamāḥ
tasmānmārgāntarāṇāṃ tu prāmāṇyaṃ vedavittamāḥ
dadāti paramāṃ muktimityepā śāśvatī śrutiḥ
vedamārgekaniṣṭhānāṃ na kiṃcidapi durlabham
ato'dhikāribhedena mārgī mānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
jagataḥ kāraṇe muktau jñānādau ca tathaiva ca
mārgāṇāṃ ye viruddhāṃśā vedāntena vicakṣaṇāḥ
te'pi mandamatīnāṃ ca mahāmohāvṛtātmanām
vāñchāmātrānuguṇyena pravṛttā na yathārthataḥ
darśayitvā tṛṇaṃ martyo dhāvantīṃ gāṃ yathāgrahīt
darśayitvā tathā kṣudramiṣṭaṃ pūrva maheśvaraḥ
paścātpākānuguṇyena dadāti jñānamuttamam
tasmāduktena mārgeṇa śivena kathitā amī
mārgā mānaṃ na cāmānaṃ mṛṣāvādī kathaṃ śivaḥ
mahākāruṇiko devaḥ sarvajño nirmalaḥ khalu
tathā'pi vedo mārgāṇāmuttamaḥ sarvasādhakaḥ
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena mārgaprāmāṇyanirṇayam
evaṃ buddhvā śrutau śraddhāṃ kurudhvaṃ yatnato dvijāḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñave
dvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
māmāṇyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi prasādakramamādarāt
yasya vijñānamātreṇa prasādaḥ śāṃkaro bhavet
purā sanatkumārākhyau muniḥ satyaparāyaṇaḥ
brahmāṇaṃ brahmasaṃpannamapṛcchadidamādarāt
so'pi sarvajagaddhātā saha tena munīśvarāḥ
nārāyaṇamanādyantamaṣṭacchadidamuttamam
so'pi nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmānsaha tābhyāmumāpatim
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhaktyā stutvā rudreṇa suvratāḥ
prāha gambhīrayā vācā viṣṇave munipuṅgavāḥ
tacchrutvā bhagavānvyāsaḥ sākṣātpratyakṣaśaṃkarāt
sanatkumārātsarvajñāduktavānmama sādaram
ahaṃ bhāgyavatāmadya yuṣmākaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
kevalaṃ kṛpayā vakṣye tadeva parayā mudā
nityakarmādyanuṣṭhānātpāpanāśo bhavatyataḥ
tayā saṃsāradopasya darśanaṃ bhavati svataḥ
tato viraktiḥ saṃsārātpunastyāgaśca karmaṇām
viriñcasya prasādena tataḥ śāntyādisādhanam
prasādādvaiṣṇavātsākṣānmumukṣutvaṃ punaḥ svataḥ
tena yogābhidhaṃ dhyānamaiśvaraṃ jñānasādhanam
punaḥ sāṃkhyābhidhaṃ jñānaṃ pārvatyāstu prasādataḥ
saṃsāramocakaḥ sākṣācchiva eva na cāparaḥ
anyāśva devatāḥ sarvāḥ praṇāyaiva hi mocakāḥ
anekajanmasaṃsiddhaḥ śrautasmārtaparāyaṇaḥ
prāyādapramādena mumukṣuriti hi śrutiḥ
prasādahetubhūteṣu praṇavākhyo mahāmanuḥ
variṣṭhaḥ kathitaḥ prājñairdevatāsu viśeṣataḥ
rudrārādhanamevoktaṃ variṣṭamiti vaidikaiḥ
oṃkārasya prasādena viṣṇoścaiva prasādataḥ
rudvārādhanavāñchā syāttadārādhanataḥ punaḥ
prasādādeva rudrasya jñānaṃ mokṣaikasādhanam
devayānābhidhā viṣṇorgatiḥ sraṣṭuḥ prasādataḥ
brāhmaṇyaṃ kīrtirindośva kherārogyameva tu
puraṃdarasya saubhāgyaṃ valaṃ vāyoḥ prasādataḥ
bhāratyāśva prasādena vāgvibhūtirayatnataḥ
kāmināṃ devatāḥ sarvāḥ sāṃsārikaphalapradāḥ
kāmanārahitānāṃ tu śuddhidvāreṇa devatāḥ
svayaṃ muktikaraḥ puṃsāṃ kāmināmacireṇa tu
svayaṃ muktikaraḥ sākṣātkāmanārahitasya tuṃ
mahādevaprasādena khalu viṣṇupadaṃ dvijāḥ
vaidikānāṃ tathā'nyeṣāmapi muktirhi sidhyati
brāhmaṇāśca vimucyante prasādena śivasya tu
kṣatriyāśva tathā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā api ca saṃkarāḥ
kiṃ punarvaidikā viprāḥ striyaḥ sarvā munīśvarāḥ
pāpaṇḍāśca vimucyante prasādena maheśituḥ
vaidikāśva kharoṣṭrādijātayaśca tathaiva ca
pāṃsavaḥ parvatāyante pāṃsūyante ca parvatāḥ
śivaprasādayuktānāmājñayaiva tu kevalam
brahmanārāyaṇādyāstu devatā akhilā api
vijāyante ca naśyanti hyājñayaiva prasādinaḥ
prasādasya ca māhātmyaṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ
api devā na jānanti śrutayaśva na saṃśayaḥ
śaṃkaro'pi mahātejāḥ śāṃkarī vā munīśvarāḥ
śivaprasādamāhātmyaṃ kiṃtu jānāti vā na vā
bhavanto'pi mahādevaprasādāya munīśvarāḥ
gurupādāmbujaṃ nityaṃ pūjayadhvaṃ yathāvalam
śrīmānapure puṇye sarvadevasamānṛte
sākṣāda sabhāmadhye nṛtyantaṃ devanāyakam
ambikāsahitaṃ nityaṃ bhajadhvaṃ parayā mudā
śrīkālahastināthasya praṇāmālokanādayaḥ
api śaṃbhoḥ prasādāya bhavanti dvijapuṅgavāḥ
vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevapraṇāmālokanādayaḥ
api śaṃbhoḥ prasādāya bhavanti dvijapuṅgavāḥ
śivaprasādena hi sarvamāstikāḥ
śivaprasādena viśuddhatā''tmanaḥ
śivaprasādastu śivaprasādataḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sutasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
trayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
prasādakamavarṇanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
atyantaśraddhayopetāḥ śṛṇutātīva śobhanam
purā kaścinmahāpāpī durghaṭo nāma nāmataḥ
jātyā śūdro mehākruddho mahāsāhasikottamaḥ
abhūttena mahāmohādvāhmaṇānāṃ śataṃ hatam
gavāṃ śataṃ hataṃ tena dagdhaṃ gehaśataṃ tathā
atha caurya kṛtaṃ tena narāṇāmavicārataḥ
balātparastriyo muktā bahuśo dṛṣṭigocarāḥ
vāpīkūpataḍāgādijalaṃ tenaiva dūṣitam
varṇāśramasaṃmācāramaryādā tena bheditā
sahasrajanmataḥ pūrve durghaṭena munīśvarāḥ
dattaṃ tena matistasya jātā kālena śobhanā
aho mohena pāpāni kṛtāni subahūni ca
mayā teṣāṃ na paśyāmi vināśasya tu kāraṇam
brāhmaṇā vedavidvāṃso vadanti narakānmama
matipradānaṃ kṛtavānbrāhmaṇaḥ kaśvidostikaḥ
śrīmadyāghrapuraṃ nāma sthānamasti mahītale
yatra nṛtyati viśvātmā śivaḥ saṃsāramocakaḥ
yasya māhātmyavijñānādviṣṇurviśvajaganmayaḥ
yasya māhātmyavijñānādvahmā viśvāmarādhipaḥ
yasya māhātmyavijñānādindraḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
yasya māhātmyavijñānāddevā yakṣāśva kiṃnarāḥ
yasya māhātmyavijñānānmunayo munisattamāḥ
yatra sarveśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādaṃ labdhavānhariḥ
yatra sarveśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādaṃ labdhavānajaḥ
yatra vajrī haraṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādaṃ labdhavāndijāḥ
yatra dṛṣṭvā haraṃ devā aśeṣā āstikottamāḥ
prasādaṃ labdhavantastu svādhikārānurūpataḥ
ityevaṃ brāhmaṇenoko durghaṭaḥ puṇyagauravāda
śrīmadvyāghrapuraṃ gatvā śraddhayā parayā saha
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā jñātvā nityamatandritaḥ
namontaṃ śivamantraṃ tu japitvā'ṣṭottaraṃ śatam
dṛṣṭvā bhūmau mahābhaktyā daṇḍavatpraṇipatya ca
śivajñānaikaniṣṭhāya dattvā dhānyaṃ dhanaṃ mudā
satyavāk śaucasaṃpannaḥ kāmakrodhādivarjitaḥ
vatsarāṇāṃ tryaṃ tatra uvāsātipriyeṇa saḥ
parapramātṛprathanaikalakṣaṇām
prasādavaibhavaṃ nāma caturviśo'dhyāyaḥ
prasādavaibhavaṃ nāma caturviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
pravakṣyāmi samāsena śṛṇuta śraddhayā saha
purā kaśvidvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutaḥ
satyasaṃdhābhidhaḥ śuddho viṣṇubhakto viśeṣataḥ
abhūttena kṛtaṃ sarva śrutismṛtyuditaṃ mudā
pratiṣṭhā ca kṛtā viṣṇorvahuśaḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ
ārādhitaśca bhagavānviṣṇurviśvajaganmayaḥ
vaiṣṇavā vividhā mantrāstena japtā dine dine
ciraṃtanāni sthānāni viṣṇordṛṣṭāni sādaram
vaiṣṇavā manujāstena pūjitāśca dine dine
punarnārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā satyasaṃdhastu prasanendriyamānasaḥ
stotumārabhate viṣṇuṃ viśvalokaikakāraṇam
viṣṇave viśvalokānāṃ hetave vividhātmane
vedavedāntaniṣṭhānāmātmabhūtāya te namaḥ
kṛṣṇāya śahantre ca mama kenāpi hetunā
pratyakṣāya prabodhāya viduṣāmātmane namaḥ
keśavāyātiśudvāya kevalāya parātmane
keṣāṃcicchuddhacittānāṃ prasannāya namo namaḥ
muñjakeśāya muṇḍāya muṇḍināmārtihāriṇe
śrīvatsāṅkāya varyāya varadāya parātmane
vañcakānāmagamyāya vastubhūtoya te namaḥ
pītavāsāya pītāya pāpapañjarahāriṇe
pāpakarmaparāṇāṃ tu bhañjakāya namo namaḥ
viṣvaksenāya viśvāya viśvotpatyādihetave
viśvavijñānarūpāya nirmalāya namo namaḥ
viśvarūpāya viśvāsalabhyāyāviditātmane
viśvottīrṇāya viśvasya sākṣirūpāya te namaḥ
murāriṇe muhūrtāya muhūrtasya vidhāyine
muhūrta bhajatāṃ nṛṇāṃ muktidāya namo namaḥ
śauriṇe śārṅgiṇe tubhyaṃ śaṃkhakundendurūpiṇe
śākamūlaparāṇāṃ tu śāntidāya namo namaḥ
hartre bhatre viśiṣṭānāmātmane viduṣāṃ namaḥ
govindāya gavāṃ nityaṃ pālakāya parātmane
bhūtanāthāya bhūtānāmādhārāya namo namaḥ
vaikuṇṭhāya viśiṣṭānāṃ viśiṣṭajñānadāyine
viśiṣṭāya viriñcādidevebhyaśca namo namaḥ
kṣīrodaśāyine sākṣātkṣīrodasyāpi hetave
nirādhārāya nityāya nityānandāya te namaḥ
yajñānāṃ pataye tubhyaṃ yajñagamyāya te namaḥ
janārdanāya daityānāṃ śatrave śaktidāyine
svabhaktānāṃ viśuddhānāṃ viśeṣeṇa namo namaḥ
vāsudevāya vasvādidāyine vāsavādibhiḥ
pūjitāya purāṇāya puṃse pūrṇātmane namaḥ
dāmodarāya devānāṃ śatrunāśaikahetave
acyutāyākhilasyāsya sākṣiṇe'cyutavastubhiḥ
haraye hārakeyūrakaṭakādivibhūṣaṇaiḥ
alaṃkṛtāya kalyāṇaśarīrāya namo namaḥ
hṛṣīkeśāya hemādidhanadhānyapradāyine
hṛdi cintayatāṃ nityaṃ namaḥ satyaparātmane
nānāvidhasya jagataḥ sthitikāraṇāya
śreyaskarāya puruṣāya namaḥ parasmai
evaṃ bhaktyā hariṃ stutvā satyasaṃdho mahādvijaḥ
iti taṃ prārthayāmāsa satyasaṃdhī janārdanam
satyavāganasūyaśca samyagjñānamahodadhiḥ
prāha gambhīrayā vācā satyasaṃdhaṃ prati dvijāḥ
nāhaṃ saṃsāramagnānāṃ sākṣātsaṃsāramocakaḥ
brahmādidevatāśvānyā naiva saṃsāramocakāḥ
śiva eva hi jantūnāṃ mahāsaṃsāravartinām
saṃsāramocakaḥ sākṣātsarvajñaḥ sāmva īśvaraḥ
tathā'pi paramā śaktirvividhā tasya śūlinaḥ
śrūyate sarvavedeṣu svajñānaṃ ca balaṃ svakam
svavyāpāraśca tasyāsya svataḥ siddho na cānyataḥ
vijñānāditrayaṃ yasmātsa eva bhavamocakaḥ
ahaṃ brahmādidevāśva prasādāttasya śūlinaḥ
praṇāyaiva hi saṃsāramocakā nātra saṃśayaḥ
prasādo muktidaḥ sākṣācchivātsatyādilakṣaṇāva
aprasaktabhavācchaṃdvādasaṅgātsarvasākṣiṇaḥ
ambikāsahitādasmātsarvajñādeva nānyataḥ
mama brahmādidevānāmapi sākṣācchivecchayā
bhogamokṣapradaḥ puṃsāṃ prasādo jāyate'nagha
tasmātprasādaśvānyeṣāṃ mama cā''śritya śūlinaḥ
prasādaṃ bhogamokṣāya na svayaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
punaḥ pūrṇaprasādāya satyasaṃdha mama priya
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ bhaja kāruṇikottamam
mahādevaṃ samāśritya vāñchitaṃ nā''pnuyādyadi
mahādevo mahādevaṃ kathamanyaṃ samāśrayet
nāmataśvārthataśvāpi mahādevo maheśvaraḥ
mahādevaṃ vinā yo māṃ bhajate śraddhayā saha
nāsti tasya vinirmokṣaḥ saṃsārājjanmakoṭibhiḥ
śivādanyaṃ parityajya śivaṃ sāmvaṃ sadā bhaja
evamuktvā hariḥ śrīmānkirīṭī garuḍadhvajaḥ
satyasaṃdho mahādhīmānmahāviṣṇoḥ prasādataḥ
parityajyākhilāndevānāśrito'bhavadīśvaram
īśvarasya prasādena satyasaṃdho mahādvijaḥ
jñānaṃ vedāntajaṃ labdhvā vimukto bhavabandhanāt
bhavanto'pi dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ śivādanyattu daivatam
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena yuṣmākaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
mama vākye'tiviśvāsaṃ kurudhvaṃ yatnato dijāḥ
prasādavaibhavaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
prasādavaibhavaṃ nāma pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi śivabhakti samāsataḥ
ekā śaṃkarasāyujyaśravā sāratarā parā
anyā śaṃkarasārūpya śradvā'tīva śivapriyā
aparā śivasāmīpyaśraddhā vedavidāṃ varāḥ
itarā śivasālokyaśraddhā'bhīṣṭaphalapradā
aparā ca śivajñāna śraddhā pāśanikṛntanī
janyā vedaśiraḥśraddhā sākṣāddijñānadāyinī
aparā śravaṇaśraddhā proktā vedāntavedibhiḥ
itarā mananaśraddhā nṛṇāṃ saṃbhāvanāpradā
anyā deveśvaradhyāna śraddhārūpā mahattarā
aparodūlanaśraddhā bhasmanā pāpanāśinī
tripuṇḍadhāraṇā tadanyā tattvadāyinī
rudrākṣadhāraṇaśraddhā cāpi bhaktirudīritā
paḍakṣarajapaśraddhā cāpi bhaktirmahattarā
śivaliṅgārcana śradvā cāpimatiranuttamā
liṅgārcanādidṛkṣā ca mahābhaktiḥ prakīrtitā
anumodanamīśasya pūjāyāṃ bhaktirucyate
pūjopakaraṇaśraddhā cāpi bhaktirudīryate
śivotsavadidṛkṣā ca śivabhaktirmahattarā
tathaivotsava sevārthamāgatānāṃ mahātmanām
annapānapradānaṃ ca śivabhaktirudīritā
mahādevakathādīnāṃ śravaṇecchā maharṣayaḥ
kathāśravaṇakāle tu śivasya paramātmanaḥ
udyānakaraṇaṃ śaṃbho śivabhaktirudāhṛtā
vāpīkūpataḍāgādikaraṇaṃ ca manīṣibhiḥ
prākāragopurādīnāṃ śivasyāmitatejasaḥ
iṣṭakādyaiśva nirmāṇaṃ śivabhaktirudīritā
śivaśāsanayuktasya pūjā śraddhā puraḥsaram
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivabhaktiparāyaṇaiḥ
śivārādhanabuddhacaiva nityānāmapi karmaṇām
naimittikānāṃ karaṇamapi bhaktiḥ śivasya tu
abhyāsaḥ śivavidyāyāstasyā adhyāpanaṃ tathā
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivaṃdṛṣṭiparāyaṇaiḥ
lekhanaṃ śivavidyāyāḥ pradānaṃ pustakasya tu
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivaśāstraviśāradaiḥ
śivapustakanikṣepasthānanirmāṇamāstikāḥ
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivadṛṣṭiparāyaṇaiḥ
śivajñānaikaniṣṭhasya maṭhikādānameva ca
annapānādidānaṃ ca śivabhaktirudīritā
śivajñānaikaniṣṭhasya śuśrūṣā śradvayā saha
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivabhaktiparāyaṇaiḥ
jāpināṃ śivamantrasya śuśrūṣā ca mahātmanām
śivayātrāparāṇāṃ tu śuśrūṣā ca tathaiva ca
śivayātrā ca vidvadbhiḥ śivabhaktiḥ prakīrtitā
śivayātrāparāṇāṃ tu bādhakānāṃ tu vādhanam
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivayātrāparāyaṇaiḥ
śivāparādhaniṣṭhānāṃ chedanaṃ parayā mudā
śivabhaktiriti proktā śivārādhanatatparaiḥ
śivajñānaikaniṣṭhānāṃ śivajñānasya suvratāḥ
dūpakasya śiraśchedaḥ śivabhaktiḥ prakīrtitā
bhasmasādhananiṣṭhānāṃ dūpakasya munīśvarāḥ
chedanaṃ śirasaḥ sākṣācchivabhaktirudīritā
viṣṇvādīnāṃ tu devānāṃ dūpakasya durātmanaḥ
viṣṇvādidevatābhaktasyeva dūpaṇakāriṇaḥ
vādhamaṃ ca mahāprājñaiḥ śivabhaktiḥ prakīrtitā
bādhanaṃ ca mahāprājñaiḥ śivabhaktiḥ prakīrtitā
āturāṇāṃ nṛṇāṃ rakṣā rakṣakāṇāṃ ca rakṣaṇam
bhītasyābhayadānaṃ ca śivabhaktiḥ prakīrtitā
sarvabhūteṣu kāruṇyaṃ priyabhāṣaṇameva ca
sarvabhūtahite śraddhā sākṣādbhaktiḥ śivasya tu
sarvabhūteṣu doṣasyādarśanaṃ guṇadarśanam
sarvabhūteṣu maitrī ca śivabhaktirudīritā
mahādeve'tiviśvāso viśvāsaḥ śivavedane
vedānteṣu ca viśvāsaḥ śivabhaktirudīritā
guruktārtheṣu viśvāso guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathā
svasya munayaḥ paramakāruṇika īśaḥ
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava
paḍiśo'dhyāyaḥ
ktivicāro nāma paḍiśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi parātparataraṃ padam
pratītāṅgītikādasmādbhūtāni munipuṅgavāḥ
utkṛṣṭāni tathā tebhyo jīvātmā cetanaḥ prabhuḥ
vyaṣṭayaśva tathā bhinnāḥ svasvabhāvānurūpataḥ
devatiryaṅmanuṣyādiśarīraṃ prāmuvanti ca
āsāṃ samaṣṭibhūtastu śreṣṭhaḥ sarvātmanā budhāḥ
tato viśiṣṭāḥ sakalā brahmaṇastu vibhūtayaḥ
tāścānyonyaṃ viśiṣṭāḥ syuryathā jīvā munīśvarāḥ
tāsāṃ brahmā'dhikastasmāddiṣṇurmukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
so'pi svavyaṣṭibhūtebhyo variṣṭhaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśva paratattvavibhūtayaḥ
rudrānandaśataṃ sarvakāraṇasya śivasya tu
kāraṇatvopalakṣyasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ
satya cinmātrarūpasya bhūmā''nanda udāhṛtaḥ
evaṃ krameṇa sarveṣāṃ jñānādhikyamapīṣyate
skandhaśākhādibhedena yathā vṛkṣo vyavasthitaḥ
utkarṣaśvāpakarṣaśca skandhaśākhādivastuṣu
tathotkarṣāpakarṣaśca rudra viṣṇvādipu sthitaḥ
taraṅgahudādīnāṃ yathā loke vyavasthitaḥ
utkarṣaśvāpakarṣaśca tathā rudrādipu sthitaḥ
viśvādhikatvaṃ rudrasya kāraṇasya śivasya ca
na vadanti janā ye te rākṣasāḥ syurna saṃśayaḥ
vyāvahārikadṛṣṭayā'yaṃ vibhāgaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
pramāṇadṛṣṭyā vastvekameva nityaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
anādṛtya mahāmohātpramāṇaṃ bhuvi mānavāḥ
mahāpāpavatāṃ nṛṇāṃ rudrādhikyaṃ na bhāsate
anekajanmasiddhānāṃ śrautasmārtānuvartinām
sopānakramato devā nṛṇāṃ saṃsāramocakāḥ
rudraḥ saṃsāramagnānāṃ sākṣātsaṃsāramocakaḥ
śiva ekaḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāramocakaḥ
vṛkṣasya mūlasekena śākhāḥ puṣyanti vai yathā
śivadhyānena devāśva tathā tṛptā bhavanti hi
ye paśyanti vimuktāste jīvanto'pi na saṃśayaḥ
so'pi mucyeta saṃsārādyathā svamaprapañcataḥ
na ca nāmāni rūpāṇi śivasya paramātmanaḥ
evamādīni nāmāni viśiṣṭāni parasya tu
viṣṇunārāyaṇādīni nāmāni parameśvare
arūpasya śivasyāpi mūrtiyā pāsakaiḥ
umārdhavigrahā śuklā trinetrā candraśekharā
nīlagrīvā parānandapramodā tāṇḍavapriyā
brahmaviṣṇumahādevairupāsyā guṇamūrtibhiḥ
tathā'pyeṣā parā mūrtirityeṣā śāśvatī śrutiḥ
taptāyaḥ piṇḍavaddimā rudramūrtiḥ parasya tu
mūrtyā tulyā'nyamūrtibhyo lakṣaṇairmunisattamāḥ
viṣṇvādīnāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ mūrtayo vyavadhānataḥ
na tulyāḥ paratattvasya mṛsa vedāntapāragāḥ
viṣṇvādīnāṃ ca devānāṃ tāni nāmāni suvratāḥ
mukhyāni na tathā'nyeṣu vyavadhānātpareṇa tu
paratattvaparijñānaṃ tasya mūrtiprasādataḥ
tatprasādaśva taddhyānapūjābhyāmeva nānyathā
annādibhojanānnṛṇāṃ yathā kṣuddinivartate
tathā mūrtiprasādena tattattvaṃ ca prakāśate
paratattvaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ svarūpamapi sarvadā
tasmānmūrtirhi sarveṣāṃ bhogamokṣaphalapradā
ato mūrti mahābhaktyā bhajadhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
parapadasvarūpavicāro nāma saptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
parapadasvarūpa vicāro nāma saptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi śivaliṅgaṃ samāsataḥ
śiva eva svayaṃ liṅgaṃ liṅgaṃ gamakameva hi
jaḍaṃ hi gamyate'nyena nājaḍaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
śivo naiva jaḍaḥ sākṣātsvaprakāśaikalakṣaṇaḥ
asvaprakāśa śvetsākṣācchivo naiva śivo bhavet
asvaprakāśaṃ kuḍyādi na śivaḥ saṃmataṃ khalu
śive'sati muniśreṣṭhāḥ svaprakāśaikalakṣaṇe
apratītaṃ bhavetsarvaṃ tataḥ śūnyamaśeṣataḥ
śūnyasiddhirapi śreṣṭhāḥ śūnyenaiva na sidhyati
khalu sarvātmanā bhānavihīnaṃ śūnyalakṣaṇam
ataḥ sākṣī śivaḥ sāmvaḥ svaprakāśakalakṣaṇaḥ
svayaṃ jyotiriti prāha śrutiḥ sādhvī maheśvaram
tasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhātītyapi cā''ha hi
taśva śaṃbhuḥ svayameva liṅgam
tataḥ śivasya liṅgamityayaṃ kho na saṃgataḥ
vahaṃkṛtiṃ cāpi manaśva buddhim
ālayaṃ liṅgamityāhurapare vedavittamāḥ
tadā'pi śaṃkaraḥ sākṣālliṅgaṃ nānyanmunīśvarāḥ
ālayo nāma cāssdhāraḥ sarvādhāraḥ śivaḥ khalu
cipaṃ hi sadā satyaṃ nācidrūpaṃ kathaṃcana
śuktikārajatādīnāmasatyatvaṃ hi saṃmatam
śuktikārajataṃ viprāḥ satya eva tataḥ śivaḥ
ataḥ kalpitarūpāṇāmādhāro bhagavāśivaḥ
janādhāro mahādevaḥ satyacaitanyalakṣaṇaḥ
jākāśasya yathā kaścinnā''dhāro vidyate dvijāḥ
paraśivaspāsskāśasvādhiṣṭhānānvaraṃ nopapadyata
vyāvartayati cā''dhāraṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ
khe mahimnīti vedāntaḥ satyavādī svataḥpramā
vedāntavākyaṃ mānānāmatimānamiti sthitiḥ
ataḥ satyacidānandalakṣaṇaḥ parameśvaraḥ
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāmajñānāndhīkṛtātmanām
cittapākāṃnuguṇyena bhāvanārthe dvijarṣabhāḥ
ādhāro mantrasaṃskārātkalpitaḥ satyavabudhāḥ
tadā'pi liṅgaṃ bhagavānsvayameva maheśvaraḥ
śuktikārajatādīnāmasatyānāṃ dvijarṣabhāḥ
layo dṛṣṭo na satyasya śuktikāśakalasya ca
līyate hi śivādanyadaśeṣamaśivaṃ śive
ato liṅgaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā avināśī heraḥ svayam
ādhāreṣu śarīre'smihiṅgāni paramātmanaḥ
adhomukhamanādyantamapiṇḍaṃ piṇḍasaṃjñitam
gurūpadeśato jñeyaṃ liṅgamekaṃ prakīrtitam
koṭisūryapratīkāśaṃ komalaṃ dvijapuṃgavāḥ
apadaṃ padamavyaktamavāṇaṃ vāṇamadbhutam
tṛtīyasthaṃ sadaivordhvamukhaṃ saṃsāranāśakam
arcanīyaṃ mahāmantrairātmaniṣṭhestu yogibhiḥ
gurūpadeśato jñeyaṃ dvitīyaṃ liṅgamīritam
candrakoṭipratīkāśaṃ śāṃkaraṃ śaktivallabham
visargādhiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ viśvavijñānasādhakam
gurūpadeśato jñeyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ liṅgamīritam
lavābhilāpairabhipūjanīyaḥ
puppatoyaphalapramukhāḥ kṛśāḥ
nālaṃ sadā mūlavimūlanāya
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ śivaliṅgasvarūpakathanaṃ
nāmāṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
nāmāṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi śivasthānaṃ samāsataḥ
purā nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmānkirīṭī garuḍadhvajaḥ
śrīmatkailāsaparyante tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ
bhasmoddhūlitasarvāṅgastripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakaḥ
rudrākṣamālābharaṇo jaṭāvalkalasaṃyutaḥ
prādurāsīnmahādevaḥ śaṃkaraḥ karuṇākaraḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣo mahādevaṃ ghṛṇānidhim
praṇamya daṇḍavatyā paramayā saha
stotramārabhate viṣṇuḥ sarvabhūtahitāvaham
akārāya namaḥ sākṣādanantānandamūrtaye
ātmabhūtāya sarveṣāmatiśudvāya śūline
ākārāyātiśudvāya sākṣiṇe sarvavastunaḥ
ikārāyeśvarākhyāya sarvasiddhikarāya ca
indrādilokapālānāmiyattākāriṇe namaḥ
īkārāya variṣṭhāya vāñchitārthapradāya ca
vañcakānāmalabhyāya vasudāya namo namaḥ
ukārāyograjantūnāmugrarūpāya śūline
uttamānāṃ tu jantūnāmupāsyāya namo namaḥ
ūkārāyopavītāya rjitāyottamātmane
ṛkārāyā''dibhūtāya rāmapūrvārcitāya ca
ṛcāmarthasvarūpāya namaḥ satyaparātmane
ṛkārāya nisargāya nityatṛptāya śaṃbhave
rasādibhūtarūpāya namaḥ śuddhacidātmane
ḷkārāya lasadgaṇḍamaṇḍitābharaṇāya ca
liṅgaliṅgayādihīnāya liṅgarūpāya te namaḥ
ḷkārāya layasthāya dhvaṃsakāyā''dihetave
lākṣāruṇaśarīrāya lābhasthānāya vai namaḥ
ekārāya namaḥ śaśvaditāsākṣiṇe tathā
ahaṃtāsākṣiṇe sākṣātpratyagaddyavastu
aikārāyāmalajñānaprabhāvapariśīlinām
ātmarūpatayā nityaṃ pratītāya namo namaḥ
okārāya viriñcāya viṣṇave rudramūrtaye
vācyavācakahīnāya svayaṃbhānāya vai namaḥ
maukārāya maheśāya mahāmantrārtharūpiṇe
mahādevāya mātrādimapañcāya namo namaḥ
vindurūpāya vījāya vījādhiṣṭhānarūpiṇe

paratattvāya tattvānāṃ tattvabhūtāya vastutaḥ
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśva īśvaraśva sadāśivaḥ
virāḍādyāśva devāśca yanmātraṃ taṃ numaḥ śivam
mahāsattvāśva ye jīvā madhyasattvācaṃ cetanāḥ
vihīnāścaiva yanmātraṃ taṃ namāmi mahaujasam
yasya sattā jagatsattārūpeṇaivāvabhāsate
yaṃ vinā na jagattasmai sadā sākṣātsate namaḥ
yasya bhānaṃ jagadbhānasvarūpeṇa vibhāsate
yamṛte na jagagānaṃ tasmai bhānātmane namaḥ
āgamā akhilā niyaṃ vande tadbrahmasaṃjñitam
tarkābhāsaistamīśānaṃ vande dehavilakṣaṇam
yatsvarūpamavijñāya dehajānīndriyāṇi tu
yatsvarūpamavijñāya prāṇamātmeti manvate
vande taṃ prāṇavettāraṃ prāṇaṃ prāṇasya sarvadā
yatsvarūpamavijñāya manaḥ saṃkalpalakṣaṇam
antaḥkaraṇamātmeti manvate taṃ numaḥ śivam
yasmiñjāgradavasthaiṣā bhātīva bhavatīva ca
taṃ tadbhrānteradhiṣṭānaṃ vande sākṣiṇamīśvaram
taṃ tadbhrānteradhiṣṭhānaṃ vande sākṣiṇamīśvaram
taṃ tadbhrānteradhiṣṭhānaṃ vande sākṣiṇamīśvaram
yasmintaṃ turīyatvaṃ tridhāmāpekṣayaiva tu
yasmiṃsturīyātītatvamadhyastaṃ tadbhāvataḥ
taṃ vande kevalaṃ śuddhaṃ nirviśeṣaṃ maheśvaram
bahutvaṃ ca tamīśānamasaṃkhyeyaṃ numaḥ śivam
taṃ sadā kevalaṃ vande keṣāṃ cillabhyamīśvaram
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sadeśvarasadāśivo
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvadevānaśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vibhinnāñjīvacetanān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvavedānaśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ smṛtīḥ sarvā aśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ purāṇāni ca bhāratam
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvāñvāgamānapi
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vividhānvaiṣṇavāgamān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā brāhmānetāṃstathā''gamān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā buddhārhatāgamānimān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ śabdānsatyetarādikān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vidyāḥ sarvā aśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāstarkāninyonyavādhakān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā mānamadhyakṣapūrvakam
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā brāhmaṇānkṣatriyānviśaḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ śūdrānapi ca saṃkarān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā āśramānakhilānapi
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā dharmādharmānaśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā varjyāvarjyānaśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vidyāvidyā aśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā dehādīnakhilānimān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā jāgradāditrayaṃ sadā
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā bhūmiṃ tadamāstikāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā jalaṃ tadvedamāstikāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā agniṃ tadvedamāstikāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vāyuṃ tadvedamāstikāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā ākāśaṃ tatra kalpitam
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ śabdasparśādikānimān
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā mahadādyakhilaṃ jagat
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvametadaśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā mahāmāyāmaśaṅkitāḥ
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāśvicchaktiṃ vimalāmimām
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ pratītamakhilaṃ jagat
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ phalāvāpyai kadācana
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ pratyagjyotiṣi saṃsthitāḥ
idaṃrūpamahaṃrūpaṃ yasya bhāti tamīśvaram
evaṃ vyāsena sarvajñaḥ sāmbaḥ sarvaphalapradaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaṃ devyā sahitamavyayam
prāha gambhīrayā vācā munaye munisattamāḥ
śṛṇuṣva śraddhayā sārdhaṃ mayā noktamitaḥ purā
apekṣitārthaḥ sarveṣāṃ bhuktirmuktiśca suvratāḥ
muktirnānāvidhā proktā mayā vedānusārataḥ
taṃtra sāyujyarūpāyā mukteḥ sākṣāttu sādhanam
nityasiddhā'thavā muktiḥ sādhyarūpā'dvayī gatiḥ
nityasiddhā tu sarveṣāmātmarūpā'thavā'parā
viśvamasya nivṛttyā sā prāpteti vyapadiśyate
ajñānasya vināśastu jñānādeva na cānyataḥ
jñānādajñānanāśastu prasiddhaḥ sarvadehinām
prāpyā cedātmanā muktiraprāptaprāptireva sā
sādhyānāmapi bhāvānāmanityatvaṃ vyavasthitam
sādhyatvākhyastu dharmaśca naivābhāvāśrayo bhavet
tadā'pi nityaprāptāyā muktaḥ prāptistu pūrvavat
aprāpyāyāstu mukteśva nāstyapekṣā hi sādhane
prāgabhāvasya sādhyatvābhāve satyapyabhāvataḥ
bhāvānāmapyabhāvānāṃ sādhyānāṃ munisattama
asādhyānāṃ ca sarveṣāmanityatve prayojakam
tasmāduktaprakāreṇa muktiḥ sāyujyarūpiṇī
jñānalabhyā kriyāmātrānna labhyā na samuccayāt
jñānaṃ nāmākhilaṃ cedaṃ sadrūpeṇāvabhāsanam
kriyā tu kārakāpekṣā na jñānālambinī sadā
jataḥ kriyāyā jñānena virodhādeva sarvadā
sārūpyākhyā tu yā muktiḥ sāmīpyākhyā ca yā'parā
sālokyākhyā ca yā tāsāṃ kevalaṃ karma sādhanam
aihikāmuṣmikākārā muktayaḥ sarvadehinām
nāstikyādeva sarveṣāṃ saṃsāre parivartanam
evamuktvā mahādevaḥ sāmbaḥ sarvāvabhāsakaḥ
muktisādhanavicāro nāmāṣṭātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
sādhanavicāro nāmāṣṭātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāt
avirodhaṃ tu vedānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ munīśvarāḥ
dvividho vedarāśistu munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
satyādvaitaparaḥ kaśvidvedabhāgaḥ samāsataḥ
abhyastaṃ hi sadā dvaitaṃ dṛśyatvācchuktirūpyavat
dṛśyatvaṃ dvaitajātasya saṃmataṃ sarvadehinām
advaitaṃ sarvadā satyaṃ bhedābhāvātkathaṃcana
advaitamapi cādhyastaṃ yadi vedavidāṃ varāḥ
vyavahāradaśāyāṃ tu satye'dhyāsasya darśanāt
dvaitādvaitātirekeṇa nāstitvādeva vastunaḥ
śūnyamātre na cādhyastamubhayaṃ vedavittamāḥ
nirupākhyasya cādhyāsāviṣṭhānatvādyasaṃbhavāt
tasmāduktena mārgeṇa kaśvidaṃśaḥ śruterbudhāḥ
satyādvaitaparaḥ proktaḥ sarvaśāstrārthavedibhiḥ
tathaiva vedurāśestu kaśvidaṃśastapodhanāḥ
dvaitādvaitaśrutīnāṃ tu virodho'pi pratītitaḥ
tatraivārthavatī sākṣādadvaitaśrutirāstikāḥ
tena nārthavatī tatra śrutirmānātigāminī
pramāṇāntarasaṃvādāpekṣā nāsti śruteḥ sadā
svataśca parato doṣo nāsti tasyāḥ śruterapi
pratyakṣādipramāṇānāṃ doṣavadbhāvatā sadā
astyataḥ śrutireteṣāṃ pramāṇānāṃ balīyasī
tatra prayojanābhāvātparamārthanirūpaṇe
ataḥ prayojanābhāvādvaitaṃ na pratipādyate
smṛtīnāṃ ca purāṇānāṃ bhāratādestathaiva ca
tathā śaivāgamādīnāṃ tarkāṇāṃ ca dvijottamāḥ
vodhayanti mudā kāśvicchūtayaḥ paṇḍiteottamāḥ
bodhayanti mudā kāścicchūtayaḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ
sādhakasyaiva jīvasya svābhāvikaśivātmatām
jīvatvaṃ cetanasyāsya svābhāvikamiti dvijāḥ
keciddadanti vārtepā na tatsvābhāvikaṃ sadā
yathā bheṣajasaṃparkāttāmrasya malanāśanam
yathā svābhāvika herauṣṇyaṃ naiva vinaśyati
prakāśo vā tathā'syāpi na duḥkhādirvinaśyati
maṇimantraupadhādīnāṃ śaktivaicitryamātrataḥ
neṣṭavatprativaddhaṃ tu na naṣṭaṃ saṃmataṃ hi tat
naṣṭayatprativaddhaṃ hi vinaṣṭaṃ manyate'budhāḥ
jīvatvaṃ ca tathā'syāpi sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇam
payasā veṣṭitaṃ toyaṃ paya ityabhidhīyate
tathā'pi mānavā śrāntāḥ kāñcanaṃ manyate hyayaḥ
sūkṣmadarśanahīnānāṃ sulabhaḥ khalu vibhramaḥ
tathā śivatvaṃ jīvasya śrānyā siddhaṃ bhaviṣyati
tato jīvaḥ śivaḥ sākṣātra bhavettu kadācana
śiva eva svataḥ sākṣācchivo bhavati nānyathā
uṣṇaṃ toyamiti prājñāḥ pratītāvapi dehinām
tathā'śivaḥ svato jīvaḥ kadācitpaṇḍitottamāḥ
ekadeśena vā jīvāḥ kiṃvā sarvātmanā samaḥ
ekadeśena cetsarve śivāḥ saṃsāravartinaḥ
sarvātmanā cetsāmyaṃ tatsarvathā śiva eva saḥ
bhedakāraṇaśūnyatvādbhedābhāvācca vastutaḥ
tasmājjīvaḥ svataḥ sākṣācchivaḥ satyādilakṣaṇaḥ
svājñānaṃ tatprasūtaṃ ca saṃsāraṃ svātmanā grasan
svapūrṇaśivarūpeṇa svayamevāvaśiṣyate
śuktikāmātrarūpeṇa yathā loke'vaśiṣyate
śivātmanā jagadbādho na caivaṃ saṃbhaviṣyati
bhāvarūpaṃ tu vastveva bhāvi bhavati dvijāḥ
jaganna bhāvo nābhāvo bhāvābhāvavilakṣaṇam
adhiṣṭhānāvaśeṣo hi kevalaṃ paṇḍitottamāḥ
jagadbhramasyādhiṣṭhānaṃ śivaḥ satyasvabhāvataḥ
tadanyadakhilaṃ bhrāntaṃ yuktitaśca pramāṇataḥ
tasmātsarvajagadvādhe śiva evāvaśiṣyate
śivāvaśeṣaṃ sarvasya jagataḥ śrutirādarāt
tasmātsatyaparānandaprakāśādvaitamīśvaram
vākyāntarāṇi sarvāṇi śepabhūtāni saṃtatam
śivasya śepaṃ sakalaṃ śrutermānāni sarvaśaḥ
yathā mātā svaputrasya satyamevābhibhāṣate
śrutau cāpi mahādeve tripuṇḍre bhasmaguṇṭhane
śraddhāṃ na kurute martyaḥ puṇyaleśavivarjitaḥ
pāpiṣṭhānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tripuṇḍrolane śrutau
tripuṇḍroḍūlanotkarṣe śraddhā puṇyavatāṃ bhavet
vedānusārismṛtyādau pāpiṣṭasya na hi spṛhā
viṣṇvādeḥ śivasāmyatve vedasāmye parasya ca
kurvantīcchā mavidvāṃsaḥ pāpamevātra kāraṇam
tathā śivāpakarṣe ca yatante pāpayonayaḥ
vyarthamityāhuratyartha pāpaṇḍāḥ pāpayonayaḥ
mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ vedānāmapi vaibhavam
tripuṇḍrasya ca māhātmyaṃ na śakyaṃ varṇituṃ mayā
karmaśeṣatvamāyāsādbrahmakāṇḍasya kecana
alpalābhapradaṃ karma jñānaṃ pūrṇaphalapradam
tathā sati muniśreṣṭhāstacchepatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
phalavāda paraṃ jñānaṃ tatastaccheṣatā'sya na
karmaprakaraṇasthaṃ hi jñānaṃ karmāṅgamiṣyate
bhinnaprakaraṇaṃ jñānaṃ tatastaccheṣatā'sya na
karma sādhyaphalaṃ brahmajñānaṃ siddhaphalaṃ budhāḥ
tathā sati muniśreṣṭhāstacchepatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
adhikārivibhedena pravṛttaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
tathā sati kathaṃ viprā jñānakarmasamuccayaḥ
aprakāśātmakaṃ karma svaprakāśaṃ tu vedanam
tathā sati kathaṃ viprā jñānakarmasamuccayaḥ
tasmāddedāntabhāgastu brahmakāṇḍasamāhvayaḥ
sarvathā karmakāṇḍasya naiva śeṣaḥ kadācana
na sākṣādeva śeṣaḥ syājjñānaṃ vedāntavākyajam
śāntidāntyādayaḥ sarve guṇā eva munīśvarāḥ
aṅgāni brahmavidyāyāḥ śravaṇaṃ karaṇaṃ budhāḥ
vidyāphalopakāri syānmananaṃ cintanaṃ tathā
jñānamajñānavicchitau na sahāyamapekṣate
tathā'jñānanivṛttau tu jñānaṃ nānyadapekṣate
kṣaṇadhvaṃsikriyāyāstu dharmādharmātmikaṃ phalam
na jñānaṃ tena vidyāyā na sākṣātkarma sādhanam
na jñānaṃ tena vidyāyā nādharmaḥ sādhanaṃ bhavet
karmaṇā śuddhacittasya saṃsṛterdoṣadarśanam
punarviraktiḥ saṃsārānmokṣecchā jāyate tathā
tasmātkarma manāyaiva jñānaśeṣaṃ na cānyathā
sutarāmeva nāstyeva samyaguktaṃ mayā'naghāḥ
viplāvayanti vedārthaṃ naiteṣāṃ matiruttamā
pratyuta bhrāntivijñānāddedāntārthasya vādhanāt
sadā saṃsāravartitvameva teṣāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
aho mohasya māhātmyaṃ sarvavedārthavarjitāḥ
iti śrī skandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava khaṇḍe vedā
nāmavirodhanirūpaṇaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
rodha nirūpaṇaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvasiddhikaraṃ nṛṇām
kāyikaṃ vācikaṃ caiva mānasaṃ ca tathaiva ca
line śivārcanaṃ caiva rudrākṣāṇāṃ ca dhāraṇam
sarvāṅgonūlanaṃ caiva tripuṇḍrasya ca dhāraṇam
vācikaṃ karma viprendrāḥ sarvasiddhikaraṃ nṛṇām
ṣaḍakṣarasya mantrasya sāvitryāśca japastathā
vedapārāyaṇaṃ caiva vedāṅgānāṃ ca kīrtanam
mānasaṃ karma viprendrāḥ sarvasiddhikaraṃ nṛṇām
mahādevasmṛtiḥ sākṣānmahādevyāḥ smṛtistathā
vedāntārthavicāraśca vedādanyatra vismṛtiḥ
śivasyotkarṣatāvṛdviḥ śivo'hamiti bhāvanā
ete dharmā viśiṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarvasiddhikarā api
cinmantrasyeti saṃvidrūpiṇyāḥ paraśaktervācako hṛllekhāmantraścinmantraḥ padā
ebhyo'tiriktā ye dharmāḥ śrautasmārtāstathā'pare
tasyāsādhāraṇā dharmā eta eva na cāpare
tasmādete hi sarveṣāṃ sarvasiddhikarā nṛṇām
sattā siddhiśva sarveṣāṃ mahādevaprasādataḥ
viṣṇvādīnāmato dharmāḥ pūrvoktāḥ sarvasiddhidāḥ
mukhato mokṣadā te pṛṣṭhataḥ sarvasiddhidāḥ
śīghra siddhikarāścaiva śivāsādhāraṇatvataḥ
bhūmidevasamo maryo yathā nāsti dvijarṣabhāḥ
yathā bhāgīrathī tulyā nadī loke na vidyate
śivasthānasamaṃ sthānaṃ yathā loke na vidyate
dvikaradharmavicāro nāma catvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
catvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi pātakāni samāsataḥ
śṛṇuta śraddhayā sārdhaṃ parihārāya suvratāḥ
pātakāni samāsena daśa proktāni sūribhiḥ
prathamaṃ pātakaṃ proktaṃ mahāpātakasaṃjñitam
dvitīyamatipāpākhyaṃ tataḥ prāsaṅgikābhiyam
jātibhraṃśakaraṃ paṣṭhaṃ saṃkīrṇakaraṇaṃ tataḥ
apātrīkaraṇa paścānnavamaṃ tu malāvaham
prakīrṇakasamākhyaṃ tu daśamaṃ pātakaṃ dvijāḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃ suvarṇasya haraṇaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
jananīgamanaṃ caiva saṃyogastaiḥ saha dvijāḥ
mahānti pātakānyāhurmunayaḥ sūkṣmadarśinaḥ
asākṣānmātṛgamanaṃ svaputrīgamanaṃ tathā
snupāyā gamanaṃ taddadbhaginīgamanaṃ tathā
śivasya mūrticalanaṃ viṣṇośca brahmaṇastathā
rajasvalāyā garbhiṇyā ārtāyāśva vadhastathā
avijñātasya garbhasya śaraṇāgatadehinaḥ
kauṭasākṣyaṃ suhṛdisā brāhmaṇasya tapodhanāḥ
bhāryābhigamanaṃ tadatmāhuḥ prāsaṅgikābhidham
mātṛṣvasurmātṛsakhyurduhiturgamanaṃ tathā
mātulānīsnupāśvabhrūgamanaṃ ca tathaiva ca
tripuṇḍradhāraṇāāvo bhūtyā'nuḍūlanaṃ tathā
puṇḍrāntarasya viprendrā dhāraṇaṃ tadvadeva tu
pāśāṅkuśagadādaṇḍaśaṅkhacakrādibhirdvijāḥ
aṅkanaṃ vigrahe santaḥ pātakaṃ prāhurāstikāḥ
bhāryābhigamanaṃ tadvatsvavadhūsakhyurāstikāḥ
caturthāśramaniṣṭhāyā nikṣiptāyāstathaiva ca
pāpaṇḍeṣu ca niṣṭhānāṃ saṃbandho dvijapuṅgavāḥ
mukhyopapātakaṃ prāhurmahānto vedavittamāḥ
asatyabhāṣaṇaṃ taddatvaiśunyaṃ rājagāmi ca
adhītāyāḥ śrutestyāgaḥ svānestyāgastathaiva ca
pitṛmātṛsvasṛtyāgaḥ svāyatyāga evaṃ ca
abhakṣyabhakṣaṇaṃ tadvatparārthagrahaṇaṃ tathā
drumagulmalatādīnāṃ hiṃsayā jīvanaṃ tathā
yajñasyākaraṇaṃ tadvatputrānutpādanaṃ tathā
asacchāstrābhigamanaṃ nāstikyaṃ ca kuśīlatā
madyapastrīniṣevā ca prāhurgeṇopapātakam
viprāṇāṃ rogakāritvamatreyantrātireva ca
surāghrātiṃ tathā jehrayaṃ paśau puṃsi ca maithunam
jātibhraṃśakaraṃ prāhurdhārmikā vedapāragāḥ
grāmyāraṇyapaśūnāṃ tu hiṃsanaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
saṃkīrṇakaraṇaṃ prāhuḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradāḥ
kusīdajīvanaṃ caiva vāṇijyamanṛtoktitā
śūdrasya yājanaṃ prāhurapātrīkaraṇātmakam
pakṣiṇāṃ ghātanaṃ cāpi jalasthalanivāsinām
madyaspṛṣṭasya bhuktiṃ ca prāhuḥ santo malāvaham
pravadanti hi vidvāṃsaḥ satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
madaṇḍadaṇḍanaṃ caiva yuddhe bhītyā palāyanam
kṣatriyasya viśeṣeṇa mahāpātakamucyate
vañcanaṃ ca tulāmāne mahāpāpaṃ viśo bhavet
