anekakoṭibhiḥ kalpairarjitaiḥ puṇyarāśibhiḥ
sthānametanmanuṣyāṇāṃ sidhyatyatyantaśobhanam
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava khaṇḍe
pāpaśuyapāyakathanaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
pakapanaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dravyaśuddhiṃ samāsataḥ
śraddhayā saha viprendrāḥ śṛṇutā''tmaviśuddhaye
ātmadravyaṃ svayaṃ śuddhaṃ satyajñānādilakṣaṇam
sattāmātre na doṣo'sti svataḥ śuddhaṃ yataḥ sadā
yadi sattā svato'śuddhā duṣṭaṃ sarve bhavetsadā
duṣṭasattābhisaṃbandhāduṣṭaspṛṣṭaṃ sadā khalu
śreṇa do pa ja 'ti nirdoṣabhāga ḍa ca 'ti nirdoṣāmā
sattāśūnyaṃ tu tucchaṃ syātsattā śuddhā svatastathā
jñaptirūpamapi jñānaṃ śuddhameva svataḥ sadā
aśuddhirjaḍarūpe hi dṛṣṭā sarvajanairapi
svataḥsphuraṇarūpaṃ tu jñānaṃ duṣṭaṃ bhavedyadi
duṣṭameva bhavetsarve duṣṭasphuraṇa saṃgamāt
duṣṭakāraṇa vijñāne doṣo'stīti vadedyadi
abhivyañjakattyā tu jñāne doṣo na ca svataḥ
anyathā sakalaṃ jñānaṃ duṣṭameva svato bhavet
ataḥ sphuraṇarūpaṃ tu jñānaṃ śuddhaṃ sadaiva tu
aśuddhaḥ sarvathā bhāvo nārśvate puruṣaiḥ khalu
ātmarūpaṃ sukhaṃ nityaṃ naiva janmavināśavat
premālambanataḥ svātmā sukhameva na saṃśayaḥ
ātmanaśca sukhasyāpi premālambanatā sadā
mataścā''tmatayā nityaṃ sukhaṃ nirdoṣameva hi
ataḥ satyacidānandaḥ svataḥ śuddho na saṃśayaḥ
satyādilakṣaṇaṃ cā''tmadravyaṃ śuddhaṃ tataḥ svataḥ
ajñānopādhisaṃparkādaśuddhamiva bhāti tat
viśuddhiḥ paramā tasya jñānādeva na karmaṇā
svataḥ śuddhasya cājñānādaśuddhiḥ svātmavastunaḥ
ajñānasya nivṛttyaiva śuddhiḥ svābhāvikī bhaveda
karmaṇā śuddhirutpannā yadi sā tasya naśyati
saccidānandarūpātmā nityaśuddhaḥ svayaṃ svataḥ
ajñānājjīvatā tasya naiva svābhāvikī sadā
ato jīveśvaraikatvajñānādevā''tmavastunaḥ
viśuddhiḥ paramā proktā karmaṇā na kathaṃcana
ajñānenā''vṛto jīvo vyavahāre tu karmaṇā
vedoditena śuddhiḥ syājjñānācchuddhiḥ parā'sya tu
anātmarūpaṃ yaddravyamaśuddhaṃ tatsvabhāvataḥ
ādhyātmikādibhedena dvidhā'nātmā vyavasthitaḥ
pṛthivyādīni bhūtāni bhautikāni tathaiva ca
śabdasparśādayaḥ proktā ādhibhautikasaṃjñitāḥ
vedoditācca saṃskārācchivabhāvanayā'pi ca
tathā hiṃsādirāhityāddehaśuddhirdvijā bhavet
indriyāṇāmadhiṣṭhātṛdevatāsmaraṇādapi
śivabhāvanayā cāpi viśuddhirdvijapuṅgavāḥ
prāṇāyāmādadhiṣṭhātṛdevatāsmaraṇādapi
śivabhāvanayā śuddhirbhavetprāṇasya suvratāḥ
niṣiddhacintanābhāvācchivabhāvanayā'pi ca
samādhau vilayaśvāpi viśuddhiḥ parikīrtitā
svātmānaṃ manvate śuddhaṃ sā śuddhirvyāvahārikī
aśuddhyā'śuddhavadbhāti śarīrādestu cetanaḥ
bhūtabhautikarūpāṇāṃ viśuddhirbrahmabhāvanāt
brahma sarvamiti jñānādbhāvanābalato'pi vā
vinā viśuddhirdravyāṇāṃ na sidhyati kadācana
śuddhiḥ kṛcchreṇa siddhā'pi dvijā vedārthapāragāḥ
aśuddhyā cāssvṛtaṃ sarve dhūmenāgniryathā''vṛtaḥ
vedasiddhena mārgeṇa śreyaskāmairmanīṣibhiḥ
caṇḍālādyaistu saṃspṛṣṭaṃ mṛnmayaṃ pakvamutsṛjet
prakṣālayedapakkaṃ tu prokṣayedā kuśodakaiḥ
pakkaṃ śūdreṇa saṃspṛṣṭaṃ prokṣaṇādeva śudhyati
tyājyamevopayuktaṃ syātpunaḥ pākena vā śuci
ākāradditayātmasthaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tu purātanam
agnidāhena saṃśudhyennūtanaṃ kṣālanena tu
viṣṭhayā mṛnmayaṃ spṛṣṭamupayuktaṃ parityajet
udakyāśucisaṃspṛṣṭaṃ yajñapātraṃ tu dāravam
upayuktaṃ tyajedanyatkṣālayeca kuśāmbhasā
annaṃ droṇādikaṃ pakvamanyādyaspṛśyadūṣitam
kṣālanena vighātena pariśuddhaṃ hi cā''padi
droṇādūnaṃ tyajedvārādadhikaṃ prokṣayedbudhaḥ
kumbhādūrdhvaṃ dvijā dhānyaṃ pakkaṃ prokṣaṇataḥ śuci
bhārādūnaḥ parityājyaḥ pakkadhānyasya taṇḍulaḥ
bhāradvayādadhaḥ kṣālyastadūrdhvaṃ prokṣaṇācchuciḥ
annaṃ pakkaṃ parityājyamudakyānyādidūṣitam
bhāraṣaṭraudanaṃ kṣālyaṃ prokṣaṇīyaṃ tataḥ param
udakyāntyādisaṃspṛṣṭaṃ vastraṃ prakṣālayettathā
śvasūkarakharoṣṭrādispṛṣṭaṃ ca kṣālayettathā
raktavastraṃ tathā kṛṣṇaṃ prokṣayetkambalādikam
taṇḍuleṣu tathā dhānye guḍe gavye rasātmake
kākādidūṣitāṃśaṃ tu tyaktvā saṃprokṣayedbudhaḥ
duṣṭabhāṇḍasthitasyāsya bhavedopo na cāparaḥ
dravyāṇāmagnipakvānāṃ dhānyavacchuddhirīritā
keśalomanakhaspṛṣṭaṃ krimikīṭādidūṣitam
annaṃ tu bhasmanā śuddhaṃ prokṣaṇena ghṛtena ca
krītaṃ piṣṭamayaṃ sarve punaḥ pākena śudhyati
śūdrāntyāśucisaṃspṛṣṭaṃ tyājyameva na saṃśayaḥ
nidhāya śaucaṃ kṛtvā'tha gṛhṇīyātmokṣitaṃ tataḥ
adbhistu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām
prakṣālanena khalpānāṃ śuddhirvedoditā'parā
taijasānāṃ surāsparśe vahnidāhena śuddhatā
brāhmaṇasya viśāṃ rājñāṃ kṣālanena viśuddhatā
śvacāṇḍālādisaṃsparśe taijasānāṃ tu mārjanāt
prokṣaṇācca viśuddhiḥ syāttintiṇyā tāmraśodhanam
bhasmanā mṛjalābhyāṃ ca mārjanena viśuddhatā
kalyāṇe tīrthayātrāyāṃ rāṣṭrakṣobhe ca saṃbhrame
śūdrānulomakākādyaiḥ pratilomaiśva dūṣitam
mṛjjalābhyāṃ viśudhyeta tvekaviṃśatimārjanāda
aśmanā nirmitaṃ pātraṃ bhasmanā sajalena tu
nirlepaṃ śudvimāpnoti tvekaviṃśatimārjanāt
abjāni śaṅkhaśuktyādidravyāṇi sakalāni tu
prakṣālanena śuddhāni bhasmanā mārjanena ca
sarvadoṣanivṛttyarthaṃ cintayetsudṛḍhaṃ sadā
brahmarūpeṇa saṃgrāhyaṃ sarve śuddhaṃ sadā bhavet
tatastadṛṣṭisaṃyuktaṃ viśuddhaṃ sakalaṃ bhavet
athavā sakalaṃ kārya tarkataśca pramāṇataḥ
kāraṇātmatayā paśyetsarvadopanivṛttaye
kāraṇaṃ sarvakāryāṇāṃ paramātmaiva netarava
pravadanti hi vedāntāḥ smṛtayaśvā''dareṇa tu
viśudvatāmeti na cātra saṃśayaḥ
dravyaśuddhivicāro nāma catuścatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
catuścatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
abhakṣyasya nivṛttyā tu viśuddhaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhavet
cittaśuddhī kramājjñānaṃ jāyate pārameśvaram
pārameśvaravijñāne sati saṃsārahetavaḥ
abhakṣyabhakṣaṇāccittamaśuddhaṃ bhavati svataḥ
aśuddhyā bhrāntivijñānaṃ jāyate sudṛḍhaṃ nṛṇām
bhrāntivijñānataḥ puṃso niṣiddhācaraṇe ratiḥ
tena saṃsāravṛddhiḥ syānna hi muktiḥ kathaṃcana
brahmakṣatrādikaṃ sarvaṃ yasya syādodanaṃ sadā
yasyopasecanaṃ mṛtyustajjñānī tādṛśaḥ khalu
brahmaṃsvarūpaṃ vijñāturjñānāttattasya bhāsate
jagadātmatayā bhāti yadā bhojyaṃ bhavettadā
yadā svātmatayā bhāti akṣitaṃ sakalaṃ tadā
mānataḥ svātmanā bhātaṃ bhakṣitaṃ bhavati dhruvam
jāgratsvaprābhidhe kāle pratatiṃ grasatīśvaraḥ
svasvarūpaṃ svayaṃ bhuṅkte nāsti bhojyaṃ pṛthaksvataḥ
astitālakṣaṇā sattā sadā brahma na cāparā
nāsti sattā'tirekeṇa kiṃcidapyāstikottamāḥ
bhavennaivātra saṃdeho nāsti māyā ca vastutaḥ
yogināmātmaniṣṭhānāṃ māyā sākṣiṇi kalpitā
sākṣirūpatayā bhāti śivajñānena bādhitā
vādhitā'pi punarmāyā bhāti diṅmohabhānuvat
tasmādabhakṣyaṃ naivāsti viduṣaḥ parayoginaḥ
ātmavijñānahīnānāṃ khalvevāakṣyamāstikāḥ
ddijānāmātmavijñānavihīnānāmiyaṃ budhāḥ
vyavasthā śaṃkareṇaiva nirmitā bhakṣyagāminī
laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuṃ grāmakukkuṭam
palāṇḍusadṛśaṃ sarve gandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ
kāmato'kāmataścaiva brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
bhūstṛṇaṃ śigrukaṃ caiva brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
khaṭṭāsaṃjñaṃ ca vārtākaṃ tathaivokharajaṃ tṛṇam
lavaṇaṃ bhūmijaṃ vipro mohenāpi na bhakṣayet
nakhaviṣkirasaṃjñaṃ ca tathā koyaṣṭisaṃjñitam
saulaṃ vahūrasaṃjñaṃ ca matsyādo naiva akṣayeva
vakaṃ caiva balākaṃ ca khañjarīṭakasaṃjñitam
kokilaṃ ca dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ pramādācca na bhakṣayet
pāṭhīnarohitāvādyau niyukto havyakavyayoḥ
rājīvānsiṃhatuṇḍāṃśca śaśakānnaiva bhakṣayet
kevalāni ca śuṣkāṇi tathā paryupitāni ca
ṛjīpapakkaṃ viprendrāḥ kadācinneva akṣayet
viṇmūtraṃ ca surāspṛṣṭaṃ sarva dravyaṃ tathaiva ca
surāspṛṣṭasya ca spṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
virāhakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ mūtraṃ vipro na akṣayeva
viḍālakākādyucchiṣṭaṃ nakulocchiṣṭameva ca
vedavāhyena saṃspṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
śakunīsaṃjñitānsarvāstathā grāmanivāsinaḥ
anirdiṣṭāṃścaikaśaphānkravyādāṃca na bhakṣayet
kalaviṅkasamākhyaṃ ca ṭiṭṭibhaṃ plavameva ca
haṃsaṃ cakrasamākhyaṃ ca sārasaṃ naiva bhakṣayet
rajjuvālaṃ ca dātyūhaṃ śukaṃ sārikasaṃjñitam
pratudājñjālapādāṃśca brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
purīpaṃ ca tathā mūtraṃ brāhmaṇo naiva akṣayet
narāṇāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca māṃsamaśvasya sattamāḥ
mahiṣasya ca māṃsaṃ ca brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
ajāvimāṃsaṃ raktaṃ ca gomāṃsaṃ ca tathaiva ca
mṛgāṇāṃ ca tathā māṃsaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayeva
māṃsaṃ pañcanakhānāṃ ca vinaiva sakalāni tu
kāmato'kāmato vā'pi brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
matsyaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dṛtispṛṣṭamājyaṃ kīlālameva ca
odanaṃ tu punaḥpakkaṃ nālikerarasaṃ tathā
anirdaśāhagokṣīramauṭramekaśaphaṃ tathā
āvikaṃ saṃdhinīkṣīraṃ vivatsāyāśca goḥ payaḥ
āraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣīṃ vinā
strīkṣīraṃ ca śramādā'pi brāhmaṇo na pivetsadā
gogajāśvādibhirghātaṃ pādaspṛṣṭaṃ ca kāmataḥ
anulomādibhiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet
uktānyetāni sarvāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ
abhakṣyāṇi mayoktāni bhakṣakāśca patantyadhaḥ
tasmādabhakṣyaṃ saṃtyajya brāhmaṇo matimattamaḥ
kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca vaiśyānāṃ bhakṣyameṣvapi vidyate
tathā'pi bhakṣaṇābhāvasteṣāmatyantaśobhanaḥ
śūdrādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāmabhakṣyaṃ naiva vidyate
tathā'pyabhakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ phalāya mahate bhavet
bhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇādeva viśuddhahṛdayaḥ pumān
pārameśvaravijñānānmucyate bhavavandhanāt
parameśvaravijñānaṃ vedādeva na cānyataḥ
āgamāntarajanyaṃ tu jñānaṃ na jñānamāstikāḥ
aṣṭādaśānāṃ vidyānāṃ vedādanyāśca sattamāḥ
vidyā vedānusāreṇa pravṛttāḥ sarvaśobhanāḥ
tathā'pi tāsu sarvāsu kaścidaśaḥ kvacitkvacit
śivāgamānusāreṇa tatprabhedānusārataḥ
viṣṇvāgamānusāreṇa tatprabhedānusārataḥ
brahmāgamānusāreṇa tatprabhedānusārataḥ
tattattantreṣu ye martyā dīkṣitā munisattamāḥ
soṃ'śastaireva saṃgrāhyaḥ sarvathā naiva vaidikaiḥ
maduktā saṃhitā sādhvī vedamānānusāriṇī
vedetarāgamādhīnaḥ kaśvideśo na vidyate
prasādaḥ śāṃkaraḥ samyagjñānasya khalu sādhanam
ato vedānusāreṇa dvijānāmātmaśuddhaye
abhakṣyamādareṇoktaṃ mayā vedārthavittamāḥ
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena kevalaṃ karuṇābalā
śraddadhānastvabhakṣyāṇi śramāddā'pi na akṣayet
abhakṣyanivṛttikathanaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāt
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti dehinaḥ
apaśyanvatsarādūrdhvaṃ na jīvati na saṃśayaḥ
araśmimantamādityaṃ raśmimantaṃ ca pāvakam
paśyannekādaśānmāsādūrdhvaṃ maryo na jīvati
rajataṃ vā suvarṇa vā viṇmūtraṃ vā vamennaraḥ
pratyakṣamathavā svane daśa māsāna jīvati
bhūtapretapiśācāṃśca gandharvanagarāṇi ca
rukmavarṇāndramānpaśyannava māsānna jīvati
sthūlo vā'pi kṛśo'kasmādbhavenmartyaḥ svayaṃ yadi
kṛṣṇavarṇo'thavā māsānaṣṭau jīvati mānavaḥ
svapādaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ paśyannagrataḥ pṛṣṭhato'pi vā
pate vā pāṃsuke vā'pi sapta māsānna jīvati
kapoto vā'tha gṛno vā kāko vā yadi mūrdhani
sthitaḥ kravyādasaṃjño vā paṇmāsena vinaśyati
gacchantī vāyasī paṅktiḥ pāṃsuvarṣe vimuñcati
'gaccheddāyasapaṅkībhiḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa vā naraḥ
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyeccaturvā pañca jīvati
udake cāpamaindraṃ vā trīṇi hauṃ vā sa jīvati
darpaṇe vā jale vā'pi pareṣāṃ vā'tha cakṣupi
aśiraskaṃ tathā''tmānaṃ paśyanmāsena naśyati
śuṣyate hṛdayaṃ yasya mastakaṃ dhūmasaṃvṛtam
adbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛpyecca mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ
ṛkṣavānarasaṃyuktarathenaiva tu dakṣiṇām
kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇāmbarāḥ khame śmāmavastradharāḥ striyaḥ
chinnaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ svakaṃ vāsaḥ svame paśyati yaḥ pumān
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ tasya gṛhe mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
nakṣatrāṇi divā paśyanrātrau cendradhanustathā
candraṃ raktaṃ tu vā kṛṣṇaṃ bhānuṃ paśyati mānavaḥ
ādityamaṇḍale paśyetsuṣiraṃ candramaṇḍale
ākāśe raktamālāṃ vā sadya eva vinaśyati
śmaśānaṃ bhasma keśāṃśca nadīṃ śuṣkī bhujaṃgamān
paśyetsvapradaśāyāṃ yastasya mṛtyurgṛhaṃ gataḥ
kṛṣṇairvikeśaiḥ puruṣaiḥ svapre yaḥ pīḍitaḥ pumān
pāpāṇaistāḍyate yastu mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ
ādityodayavelāyāṃ pratyakṣaṃ yasya vai śivāḥ
śokamohau sadā yasya mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ
cakṣurekaṃ sravedyasya karṇau sthānācca bhraśyataḥ
yasya nāsā ca cakrā syānmṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ
yasya jihvā ca kṛṣṇā syātsumukhaṃ durmukhaṃ bhavet
gaṇḍe ca kṛṣṇe rakte vā mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ
muktakeśī hasangāyannṛtyangacchati dakṣiṇām
diśaṃ svapre'sya mṛtyuḥ syādīdṛśasvapradarśinaḥ
śvetabhūtāstathā śvetā aśvāḥ śvetatarā api
utarāsabhasaṃyuktaṃ rathamāruhya dakṣiṇe
ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇe jyotirnatre na paśyati
ūrdhvadṛṣṭistathā raktakṛṣṇadṛṣṭiśva yaḥ pumān
ūṣmāvihīnadehaśca tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
nābhau vā hṛdaye vā'pi suṣiraṃ yasya bhāsate
yasyātyuṣṇaṃ bhavenmūtraṃ tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
jāgratkāle'thavā svapne yo'dṛṣṭena nihanyate
agnau yo nipatetsvapre yo vā naṣṭasmṛtiḥ sadā
yāmyaśabdaṃ ca yo brūyāttasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
śuklaṃ prāvaraṇaṃ raktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vā yasya bhāsate
evamādīnyariṣṭāni bhāsante yasya dusthitam
śrīmaddārāṇasīṃ gatvā snātvā gaṅgājale naraḥ
dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaraṃ devaṃ japetpañcākṣaraṃ sadā
somanāthaṃ mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīparvate'thavā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrīmallikeśvaram
bhasmanonūlya mantreṇa sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīkālahastināthaṃ vā suvarṇamukharījale
snātvā dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
goparvate tathā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā śaktīśvarābhidham
bhasmanoḍhūlya mantreṇa sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīmadṛdvācale vā'pi snātvā muktājale naraḥ
dṛṣṭvā vṛddhācaleśānaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīmadrāmeśvare vā'pi snātvā tatra mahodadhau
dṛṣṭvā rāmeśvaraṃ devaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīhālāsye'thavā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā hālāsyanāyakam
yathāśakti dhanaṃ dattvā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
vedāraṇye'thavā snātvā vedatīrthe mahodadhau
vedāraṇyādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīmahalmīkasaṃjñe vā kṣīrakuṇḍajale naraḥ
snātvā dṛṣṭvā maheśānaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
jagāraṇye'thavā snātvā kāveryāmeva mānavaḥ
gajāraṇyādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
japyeśvaraṃ tu vā gatvā snātvā kāverikājale
dṛṣṭvā japyeśvareśānaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
athavā dakṣiṇāvarte snātvā kāverikāle
dakṣiṇāvartanāśaṃ dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
kumbhakoṇe'thavā srātvā kāveryāmeva mānavaḥ
kumbhakoṇādhipaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
madhyārjane vā kāveryāṃ srātvā martyaḥ samāhitaḥ
madhyārjanādhipaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
śrīmadropatīrthe vā tathā maṅgalavaṃśake
śrīmadagnīśvarākhye vā koṭihāsye'thavā naraḥ
āmratīrthe dṛtisthāne vetāraṇyasamāhvaye
srātvā dattvā yathāśakti dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ tilaṃ tu vā
dṛṣṭvā maheśvaraṃ bhaktyā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet
athavā mānavaḥ śīghraṃ gatvā vyāghrapuraṃ mudā
śivagaṅgābhidhe tīrthe snātvā dattvā yathābalam
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā śrīmaddaśrasabhāpatim
dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ satāraṃ sarvadā japet
asminvyāghra pure puṇye yo vā ko vā tu mānavaḥ
mamāra paramā muktiḥ siddhā tasya na saṃśayaḥ
mahāpātakasaṃghāśca sthānasyāsya praveśanāva
naśyanti darśanādeva muktiḥ siddhā sabhāpateḥ
mahākāruṇiko devo mahānandaparāyaṇaḥ
yatra nṛtyati taṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate bhavabandhanāt
deśadarśanamātreṇa vimuktā bahavo janāḥ
avimuktādapi śreṣṭhamidaṃ sthānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
atra darśanamātreṇa muktiḥ siddhā hi dehinām
tatra naṣṭasya martyasya tataḥ śreṣṭhamidaṃ puram
śrīmadvyāghrapuraṃ muktvā yo vā vārāṇasīṃ gataḥ
tatra naṣṭo'pi kaivalyaṃ prāpnuyānnaiva mānavaḥ
pārvatī paramā śaktiḥ śrīmavyāghrapure sadā
prakāśate hi vidyābhiḥ saṃvṛtā karuṇāvalāt
sarvavidyālayā devī yatrātīva prakāśate
mṛtyusūcakavivaraṇaṃ nāma paṭcatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
caka vivaraṇaṃ nāma paṭcatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi pāpasyākaraṇāya tu
bhogāvaśiṣṭapāpānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ munisattamāḥ
brahmahā kṣayarogī syātsurāpaḥ śyāvadantakaḥ
svarṇāpahārī kunakhī duśvarmā gurutalpagaḥ
anukīrtanakṛnmayaḥ kharasvāmī bhavetsadā
bhagaṃdarī gurorājñābhaṅgakārī na saṃśayaḥ
gurumātsarya kṛnmaryo vikrimiḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ
guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇe'sako duṣprajñaḥ syāttu mānavaḥ
viṣṇudrohī naraḥ sākṣātkṛkalāsatvamāpnuyāt
vedāntadūpakaḥ sākṣātpulkasaḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ
unmatto vedavijñānadūpakaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ
rajasvalābhigantā syādantyajātistu mānavaḥ
kūṭakṛnmukharogī syātkūṭasākṣī tathaiva ca
kūṭakṛtyasahāyaśva tadupāyaprado'pi ca
akṣirogī bhavennityaṃ bhāryā tyāgī tu mānavaḥ
patnīvahutve tvekasyāṃ ramate paṇḍha eva saḥ
annāpahārī mandāgnirjihārogī bhavettathā
parvamaithunakṛnmartyaḥ pramehī syānna saṃśayaḥ
tathā'tithiparityāgī bhavennātra vicāraṇā
svātmotkarṣaparo nityaṃ vāmanaḥ paṅgareva ca
gonnaścaiva kṛtaghnaśca jātyandhaḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ
niḥsnehakaḥ svabhāryāyāṃ galagaṇḍī bhavennaraḥ
veśyā sevāparo martyaśchinnaliṅgo na saṃśayaḥ
piśunaḥ pūtivaktraḥ syānnarastāmrādivikrayī
eḍakojagajāśvādivikretā vyādha eva hi
jñānāpahārī mūkaḥ syānmantracorastathaiva ca
abhakṣyabhakṣako maryo gaṇḍamālī bhavetsadā
raṅgopajīvī kumatirbhavennātra vicāraṇā
andhaḥ pustakacoraḥ syāttathā syāllekhanīharaḥ
sadā puṇyakathākṣepī vakranāso bhavennaraḥ
śiṣṭācārasya dharmasya dūpako rākṣaso bhavet
jñānayogagurudeṣṭā vakrāsyo devadūṣakaḥ
devadravyāpahārī syānmanuṣyo vāyubhakṣakaḥ
taṭākārāmabhettā syādaṅgahīnastu mānavaḥ
maryādābhedako dāso bhavennātra vicāraṇā
paradārābhigāmī tu vātarogī bhavennaraḥ
madhupramehī coṣṭrādigantā nātra vicāraṇā
pativratābhigantā tu sūkaraḥ syāttu mānavaḥ
parāpavādanirato vyasanī cālasaḥ sadā
atipātakadoṣeṇa bhaveyuḥ krimayo narāḥ
tathā pātakadopeṇa virāho na saṃśayaḥ
upapātakadoṣeṇa tathā śvānaḥ sadā naraḥ
mahāpātakapūrvaiśva pātakairakhilaiḥ sadā
svasvarūpāparijñānādvadhyate khalu mānavaḥ
naiva dehādisaṃghātaḥ paṭavadṛśigocaraḥ
dṛśyarūpeṇa yadrūpaṃ dṛśyate dehapūrvakam
dṛśyatvaṃ dehapūrvasya saṃmataṃ sarvadehinām
tarhi darśanarūpeṇa pariṇāmī bhaveddhi saḥ
pariṇāmī na cā''tmā syātsarvathā mṛttikādivat
ciddihīnaṃ jaḍa naiva vibhāti munipuṅgavāḥ
svataḥ prakāśahīnasya prakāśo nopapadyate
citprakāśātmasaṃbandhādapi cetyaṃ na āsate
yā dṛgdṛśyatvahīnā sā sarvadā bhāsate khalu
sā kadācitra bhātīti yadi syānmunipuṅgavāḥ
tarhi bhānaṃ hi nābhātaṃ tejjñānaṃ bhānameva hi
bhānaṃ bhānāntareṇaiva na bhāti dvijapuṅgavāḥ
bhānarūpeṇa bhānaṃ tu sadaikaṃ na hi tadvayam
bhātaṃ ānaṃ sadā svena bhāsā bhāti na cānyataḥ
ataḥ sarvasya sākṣyasya sākṣibhūtaḥ svayaṃprabhaḥ
grūpaṃ dṛśyasaṃvaddhamiti vaktuṃ na śakyate
saṃbandhasyāpi sākṣyatvātsaṃbandho dṛśyavastugaḥ
dṛśyabhūtasya rajjvādeḥ khalu dṛṣṭastu saṃgamaḥ
asaṅgo hyayamityevaṃ bravīti ca parā śrutiḥ
cidrūpasyā''tmanaḥ sākṣādvahmatāmāha hi śrutiḥ
brahmaṇaḥ karmasaṃbandhābhāvaṃ cā''ha parā śrutiḥ
tasmādātmā svamohena saṃsārīva prakāśitaḥ
varṇāśramavayovasthāviśeṣānātmavibhramāt
adhyasyāśeṣavedānāṃ niyojyaḥ syānna ca svataḥ
ajñānādanyathā jñānaṃ manuṣyatvādimānayam
ātmā tu paramātmā'pi karmabhirbadhyate'vaśaḥ
svātmanaḥ sarvasākṣitvaṃ dehādevrvyatiriktatām
sarvasākṣiṇamātmānaṃ varṇāśramavivarjitam
ataḥ svātmāparijñānāddehe'haṃbhāvamāśritaḥ
karoti sarvaśāstroktaṃ na jñānī na hi saṃśayaḥ
īdṛśī paramā vidyā śāṃkarī bhavanāśinī
prasādādeva jantūnāṃ śaktereva hi jāyate
vāguḍūtā parā śaktiryā cidrapā parābhidhā
vande tāmaniśaṃ bhaktyā śrīkaṇṭhārdhaśarīriṇīm
icchāsaṃjñā ca yā śaktiḥ paripūrṇaśivodarā
vande tāmādareṇaiva mameṣṭaphaladāyinīm
śaktiryā paramā sākṣādvījabhūtā'khilasya ca
vande tāmaniśaṃ bhaktyā nakulīśaśivānvitām
ūrdhvarūpā'pyadhorūpā tathā'dhasthāpi madhyagā
madhyarūpā'pi cāntasthā yā tāṃ vande varapradām
vinyāsairvarṇasaṃkṛtairviśvavidyālayātmanā
vidyotamānā yā vāci vande tāmādareṇa tu
ekadhā ca dvidhā caiva tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitā
dvātriṃśadbhedabhinnā ca yā tāṃ vande parātmadām
akārādikṣakārāntairvarṇaratyantanirmalaiḥ
aśepaśabdairyā bhāti tāmānandapradāṃ numaḥ
lakṣmīvāgādirūpeṇa nartakīva vibhāti yā
tāmādyantavinirmuktāmahaṃ vande varānanām
brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca yasyā eva samudratāḥ
mahadādiviśeṣāntaṃ jagadyasyāḥ samudratam
gurumūrtidharāṃ gṛhyāṃ gṛhyavijñānadāyinīm
guhyabhaktajanaprītāṃ guhāyāṃ nihitāṃ numaḥ
